### §D.0.G — How to Use This Guide

```yaml
navigation_patterns:
  pattern_1_topic_query:
    example: "Tell me about the Lakshmi Yoga"
    procedure:
      - Step 1: Search §D.0.E for "Lakshmi Yoga" → returns [SIG.08, YOG.01.A, DSH.01.A, SAH.01, INT.03]
      - Step 2: Jump to each canonical location via line numbers in §D.0.B
      - Step 3: Read those sections; synthesize

  pattern_2_id_lookup:
    example: "What is SIG.06?"
    procedure:
      - Step 1: Search §D.0.F signatures_SIG_01_to_15 → SIG.06 = "D9 12H Gemini stellium..."
      - Step 2: Jump to §D.2 (line 477), find SIG.06 subsection
      - Step 3: For cross-references, check XRF.01 in §D.9 (line 4428)

  pattern_3_timing_query:
    example: "What happens astrologically in July 2026?"
    procedure:
      - Step 1: Jump to §D.5 (line 948) Temporal Heatmap
      - Step 2: Locate July 2026 row with DAS score + planetary events
      - Step 3: Check §D.0.E for any relevant topics ("Jupiter exaltation", "eclipses", "Rath Yatra")
      - Step 4: Jump to those sections

  pattern_4_intervention_query:
    example: "Which gemstone should I wear?"
    procedure:
      - Step 1: Jump to §D.7 (line 3778) specifically INT.02 (line 3871)
      - Step 2: Read 14-factor switching framework
      - Step 3: Cross-reference INT.01 (line 3798) for timing
      - Step 4: Cross-reference KAK.01 (line 3028) for Iron Ring continuity guidance

  pattern_5_contradiction_resolution:
    example: "What contradictions does the chart carry?"
    procedure:
      - Step 1: Jump to §D.4 (line 835) for full CTR.01-CTR.07 catalog
      - Step 2: For each contradiction, §D.4 provides resolution strategy
      - Step 3: Cross-reference related sections via XRF.01 in §D.9 (line 4428)

anti_patterns_to_avoid:
  - "Reading the document end-to-end when a specific section would suffice"
  - "Treating sections as independent without checking XRF.01 for cross-references"
  - "Citing v6.0 IDs (PLN.*, SBL.*, etc.) without jumping to the canonical v6.0 source file first"
  - "Asking about a topic not found in §D.0.E without first searching the document — it may be catalogued under a different phrasing"
```

```yaml

  pattern: signal_centric

    convergences across multiple sections and lose the depth. Signal-centric

critical_caveats:
  - "Shadbala inputs in v6.0 are taken as authoritative. Shadbala totals sum the published component values but a small number of component sums do not arithmetically reconcile to the published totals (e.g., Sun total Sthana Bala sums to 252.99 vs published 191.49).   - "The Varshphal Year Lord (VRS.YEAR.LORD) and Mudda Dasha (VRS.MUDDA.DASHA) are not populated in v6.0. Varshphal-derived timing is therefore partial; conclusions draw only on VRS.MUNTHA.SIGN = Libra and VRS.MUNTHA.LORD = Venus."
  - "The D9 Lagna per v6.0 §3.5 is Cancer. This is used consistently throughout. If the D9 Lagna is disputed in any future data revision, all §3.5 dependencies (NBRY derivation, 12H stellium counting, Karakamsa analysis, foreign-income architecture) must be re-examined."
```

## §D.4 — CONTRADICTION REGISTRY

<!-- Top 7 system-level contradictions. Each is a finding, not a bug to resolve. -->

```yaml
- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.01
  systems_involved: [Shadbala, Ashtakavarga (Shuddha Pinda)]
  fact_A: "SBL.TOTAL.SATURN rank 2 (7.47 Rupas, near-max Uccha Bala 59.18/60)"
  fact_B: "AVG.SHP.SATURN rank 7 (LAST, 80 points = Rasi 44 + Graha 36)"
  tension_type: "dignity_gap vs bindu-support gap"
  resolution_finding: >
    Saturn has the HIGHEST positional-dignity score possible (Libra exaltation, Kendra) but the LOWEST
    benefic-bindu-support in the entire planetary set. This means: Saturn-events are structurally POWERFUL
    (Uccha/Kendra/AmK) but the native's cumulative karmic "permission field" for Saturn-delivery is thin.
    Interpretation: Saturn delivers results as dramatic inflection points rather than as cumulative
    compound gains. The Mercury MD (Shuddha Pinda rank 3, SAV 54) buffers this; the Ketu MD starting
    2027-08-21 will NOT buffer it. The Saturn AD (currently running) is strength-heavy but
    bindu-light — high-impact but narrow-window delivery.

- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.02
  systems_involved: [Shadbala, Vimsopaka Bala]
  fact_A: "SBL.TOTAL.MOON rank 3 (7.26 Rupas, above minimum 6.00)"
  fact_B: "VIM Moon rank 7 (LAST, 9.1 — the only sub-10 Vimsopaka)"
  tension_type: "D1-strength vs varga-strength gap"
  resolution_finding: >
    The Atmakaraka is strong in D1 composite but weakest across divisional charts. Classical interpretation:
    Moon's D1 strength is the "surface" lighting of the personality and emotional infrastructure; its
    weakness across vargas indicates that the karmic purpose Moon-as-AK is meant to deliver is buried /
    scattered / latent — discoverable only through sustained spiritual/foreign/dissolution channels (the
    Chalit-12 delivery). The AK being Vimsopaka-weak is a classical "seeker-at-the-threshold" signature;
    it resolves through Ishta-Devata worship (Mahalakshmi per DEV.ISHTA, or Jagannath per operational
    framework) rather than through direct Moon-strengthening alone.

- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.03
  systems_involved: [Vimsopaka, Uccha Bala]
  fact_A: "VIM.1 Jupiter rank 1 (12.1 — dominant across vargas)"
  fact_B: "SBL.UCHA Jupiter rank 7 (LAST, 8.40/60 — near debilitation strength)"
  tension_type: "dispersed-strength vs positional-weakness"
  resolution_finding: >
    Jupiter has the highest multi-varga dispersion of strength (12.1 Vimsopaka = dominant across 16 charts) but
    one of the weakest Uccha Bala scores. This means Jupiter is far from exaltation (Cancer) by degree but
    holds positional advantage across nearly every divisional. Interpretation: Jupiter delivers
    structurally-stable medium-amplitude results across EVERY life domain, rather than explosive results
    in any single domain. This is a "broad-but-not-peak" karaka. Jupiter MD is far in the future
    (not in 36-month window), but Jupiter transits (esp. 2026-06-02 Cancer ingress exalted) will
    amplify the dispersed strength into temporary positional peaks.

- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.04
  systems_involved: [Rashi house placement, Chalit (degree-delivery)]
  fact_A: "PLN.MOON Rashi 11 (Gains house)"
  fact_B: "CKS.MOON Chalit 12 (Foreign/Loss/Dissolution house)"
  tension_type: "sign-placement vs degree-placement"
  resolution_finding: >
    The ENTIRE reading of the Moon (and therefore of the AK, the Sthira Matru, and the chart's emotional
    delivery) flips on whether you read Rashi-11 or Chalit-12. Per v6.0 house-system convention (Sripathi,
    Bhava Chalit) and per the §0 rule "Rashi primary for yoga/aspect; Chalit primary for transit-trigger
    and outcome delivery" — both readings are authoritative for different questions. For timing and
    outcome delivery, Moon is in the 12th: gains arrive via foreign / invisible / dissolution channels.
    For classical yoga computation (Kemadruma cancellation, Chandra Adhi Yoga testing, Gaja Kesari testing),
    Moon is in the 11th. The Chalit-12 is an additional 12° of drift from the 11H cusp (CDL.MOON),
    which is substantial — this is not a borderline case.

- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.05
  systems_involved: [D1 dignity, D9 dignity]
  fact_A: "PLN.SATURN D1 Libra = EXALTATION"
  fact_B: "D9.SATURN D9 Aries = DEBILITATION"
  tension_type: "divisional-chart polarity reversal"
  resolution_finding: >
    Saturn is both the most-exalted D1 planet (Uccha 59.18) and a debilitated-in-D9 planet. The D9 debility
    is cancelled via Neecha Bhanga (Sun in D9 Lagna Cancer as exaltation-lord of Aries). This is textbook
    "NBRY high-peak" signature — classical tradition assigns to this configuration the meaning "delayed
    but unusually high eventual delivery" in the Saturn-ruled domains (discipline, authority, structure,
    longevity, public office). The NBRY requires the SUPPORTING planet (Sun) to be intact — Sun is Shadbala
    rank 1 and in D9 Lagna — which confirms the cancellation is operationally strong. Saturn AD
    (2024-12-12 → 2027-08-21) is the first major Saturn-dasha since this cancellation architecture
    aligned with a live transit, and the transit (Saturn in Pisces/Aries) crosses Saturn's own natal
    11H-axis.

- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.06
  systems_involved: [Shadbala arithmetic]
  fact_A: "Sum of published Sthana-Bala components for Sun: UCHA 33.99 + SAPT 97.50 + OJAY 0.00 + KEND 60.00 + DREK 1.00 = 192.49"
  fact_B: "SBL.STHANA.TOTAL.SUN published value = 191.49"
  tension_type: "published-total-vs-component-sum arithmetic discrepancy"
  resolution_finding: >
    RESOLVED IN v1.1: The component sum 192.49 is arithmetically correct. The published total 191.49 is off by
    exactly 1.00 Virupa — the magnitude of the DREK Bala component itself. The most parsimonious explanation is
    that the DREK Bala contribution (1.00 Virupa) was double-subtracted or dropped in one rounding pass during
    v6.0 generation. The CORRECT Sun Sthana Bala = 192.49 Virupa; CORRECT Sun Total Shadbala = 510.32 Virupa
    (adjusted) vs 509.32 published. Rank ordering is unaffected (Sun remains #1 by > 60 Virupa over Saturn),
    and the 6.00 Rupa minimum threshold is comfortably cleared either way (8.52 Rupas corrected vs 8.51 published).
    No downstream RPT.* analysis changes. The finding is preserved as a v6.0-data-quality flag rather than
    silently corrected in the report's numeric tables, per §B.1 rule (surface-v6.0-as-authoritative).
  resolution_status: ARITHMETIC_RESOLVED
  downstream_impact: NONE (ranks and thresholds unaffected)
  v6.1_recommendation: "Fix DREK Bala arithmetic pass; audit all planets' Sthana-Bala component-sum vs published-total"

- contradiction_id: RPT.CTR.07
  systems_involved: [v6.0 Sade Sati labeling, Real-time Lahiri ephemeris]
  fact_A: "TRS.SS.C2.P5 labels 2025-03-30 through 2027-06-02 as 'Setting (Pisces)' continuously"
  fact_B: "Lahiri ephemeris shows Saturn enters Aries ~2026-03-29, retrogrades back to Pisces ~2026-08-29, direct 2026-12-11 in Pisces, re-enters Aries ~2027-04-17"
  tension_type: "aggregated-phase-label vs actual-sign-occupancy"
  resolution_finding: >
    The v6.0 Sade Sati table collapses Saturn's retrograde loops into a single 'Pisces Setting' phase
    because for Aquarius-Moon natives, both Pisces (2nd from Moon) and Aries (not a Sade-Sati sign) are
    outside the Peak zone — so for SADE-SATI-CLASSIFICATION purposes, the label remains 'Setting' so long
    as Saturn is not back in Aquarius. However, for Saturn-transit-degree-hit timing (eclipse overlays,
    Kakshya zone activation, dasha-transit synchrony), the ACTUAL sign matters. This report uses
    ephemeris positions for the Temporal Heatmap's Saturn-sign column and preserves v6.0 phase labels
    in a separate column. The contradiction resolves by using BOTH, not by overwriting either.
```

### Activation Tier Legend

| tier | DAS range | description |
|---|---|---|
| dormant | 0–39 | no major dasha/transit convergence, baseline chart operation |
| baseline | 40–59 | one weak signal, everyday karmic activity |
| elevated | 60–74 | two to three systems converging on life-area activation |
| peak | 75–89 | four or more systems converging, major life-events likely |
| critical | 90–100 | five-plus systems AND at least one system-level regime change (MD/AD change, eclipse on natal sensitive point, Chara MD sign-change) |

## §D.6 — ADAPTIVE SECTION TREE

### RPT.STR.01 — Structural Foundations: Lagna, Moon, Sun, Atmakaraka

#### STR.01.A — Lagna Integrity (Aries 12°23'55", Ashwini Pada 4)

**[L0 → L4]**

Lagna in Aries 12°23' is firmly in the heart of the sign (not Sandhi, not Gandanta). The Lagna nakshatra is Ashwini — pada 4. Ashwini pada 4 falls in Scorpio Navamsa; the pada-ruler is Mars (Ashwini ruler) operating through a Scorpio-Navamsa-flavor — an intense, transformative, penetrative quality layered on the Aries pioneering base. The Lagna lord Mars sits in the 7th house (kendra from kendra, a classical "Chamara-adjacent" configuration) but in Libra (enemy sign of Mars, Venus-ruled) and conjunct exalted Saturn within 7°38' orb `[src: PLN.MARS, PLN.SATURN, ASP.W.MARS_SATURN, HSE.7]`.

The Lagna is UNOCCUPIED by any planet, which classical tradition (BPHS Ch.9) treats as a "pure lagna" that takes its character entirely from its Lord and from planets aspecting it. The aspects on Lagna Aries are:

| Aspector | Aspect Geometry | Weight |
|---|---|---|
| Mars (1L from 7H) | 7th aspect (self-return) | L2 own-lord self-regard |
| Saturn (10L from 7H) | 7th aspect on Aries | L2 Raja Yoga constituent (10L aspects Lagna) |
| Jupiter (9L from 9H) | 5th aspect on Aries | L2 Raja Yoga constituent (9L aspects Lagna) |

The 1L + 10L + 9L all reach Lagna by aspect from 7th or 9th — this is a **triple-lord-aspect configuration** that BPHS classifies as a sustained-Raja-Yoga influence on the Self axis. The fact that Mars and Saturn BOTH sit in the 7th sending their 7th aspect back to Lagna is the classical signature of "self formed by opposition" — the self crystallizes through dealing with authorities, partners, and structural adversaries.

Ashwini pada 4 sub-factors:
- Ashwini ruler Ketu (not Mars — nakshatra lords: Ashwini = Ketu per Vimshottari assignment)
- Lagna star lord per KP = Ketu (KP.CUSP.1 Star Lord = Ketu); Sub Lord = Mercury; Sub-Sub = Mars
- **KP cuspal interpretation**: Self is signified through Ketu (moksha, foreign, detachment, isolation, occult) > Mercury (trade, communication) > Mars (action, assertion)
- This KP chain aligns with the project's foreign-income architecture: the SELF itself, at the cuspal level, points to Ketu (foreign/dissolution) as primary signifier, Mercury (trade/MD lord) as secondary, Mars (Lagna lord action) as tertiary

#### STR.01.B — Moon Integrity and Atmakaraka Analysis

**[L0 → L6]**

The Moon is the Atmakaraka (KRK.C.ATMA, Jaimini highest-degree 27°02'48"). Its operational architecture:

| Dimension | Value | Classical meaning |
|---|---|---|
| D1 Sign | Aquarius | Saturn-ruled fixed air |
| D1 Nakshatra | Purva Bhadrapada pada 3 | Aja Ekapada (one-footed goat), Ugra (fierce) category |
| Rashi House | 11 | Gains, network, elder siblings, aspirations |
| **Chalit House** | **12** | **Foreign / loss / dissolution / investment / moksha** |
| D9 Sign | Gemini | **D9 12th from D9 Lagna Cancer = foreign-income architecture seat** |
| D9 Karakamsa | Gemini | Karakamsa in 12th is an exceptional placement for spiritual/foreign/moksha signatures (classical: "moksha karakamsa") |
| Shadbala | 7.26 Rupas (rank 3, above min 6.00) | Structurally strong |
| Vimsopaka | 9.1 (rank 7, LAST) | Weakest across vargas |
| Uccha Bala | 38.02 (rank 2) | High — Moon placed close to its exaltation path |
| Avastha | Susupta / Mrat / Shant | Deep-sleep / dead / peaceful — dormant but at rest |

The **Chalit-12 Moon delivery** is the central operational fact of this chart. Moon is 12.21° from its Chalit-house cusp (CDL.MOON), a significant drift that cannot be read as borderline; Sripathi-system functional delivery is firmly 12H. Combined with:
- Moon as 4L (Cancer) in Chalit-12 = "mother/home/heart significator delivering through foreign/dissolution channel"
- Moon as AK in Chalit-12 = "soul signifier delivering through foreign/moksha channel"
- The D9 Karakamsa (AK in D9) in the D9 12H Gemini reinforces this at the dharma-chart level

The Moon's two disposal chains are worth tracing:
1. **Rashi chain**: Moon in Aquarius → ruled by Saturn (in Libra 7H exalted — terminal dispositor is STRONG) — a closed two-step chain through the AD lord. Disposition-via-AD is a rare temporal alignment.
2. **D9 chain**: D9 Moon in Gemini → ruled by Mercury (in Capricorn 7th from D9 Lagna, Vargottama, Kendra) — again a strong terminal dispositor, and that dispositor is the active MD lord.

Both the Moon's dispositor chains terminate in the two planets currently running the Mahadasha/Antardasha (Mercury MD + Saturn AD). This is an extraordinary temporal convergence: the AK's structural fate lives inside the active dasha pair. This remains operative until 2027-08-21 when Mercury MD ends.

**Classical interpretation of Moon AK in D9 12H** (per Jaimini tradition and Sanjay Rath corpus): the soul-purpose of the native lives in the 12H-signified domains — dissolution of self into something larger, isolation/retreat, foreign residence, moksha through service, or large-scale investment/asset accumulation that remains out-of-sight (not 2H visible wealth, not 11H visible networks, but 12H invisible-and-compounding). The classical warnings attached: 12H-AK natives often feel misunderstood by family/society in mundane matters; their real delivery is "behind the curtain."

**[L5 Contradiction]** The tension: a 12H-AK with a Chalit-11-to-12 drift AND D9-12H stellium AND Mercury-Vargottama dispositor-from-kendra is structurally consistent — it says the same thing four ways. The contradiction is with the Avastha: Moon in Susupta/Mrat/Shant (dormant). The mechanism is strong, the living activation of it is dormant. This is where Mercury MD's 17-year Yogi-aspect and the upcoming Saturn-Yogini (2026-12 onwards) are supposed to AWAKEN the mechanism that the Avastha records as sleeping.

**[L6 Intervention leverage]** Derived from Moon-as-AK-in-D9-12H:
1. **Ishta Devata worship** — Mahalakshmi per classical derivation (12H from D9 AK Moon = Taurus → Venus → Mahalakshmi). This is not optional for a 12H-AK; it is the structurally-specified devata intervention.
2. **Pearl (Moon gemstone)** — must be worn with the Chalit-12 delivery in mind; i.e., to activate the foreign/dissolution-channel gains. The memory-framework specification (pearl Apr 20 ingestion, Monday, Moon exalted Taurus with Rohini nakshatra) aligns with activating Moon in its exaltation-sign territory (Taurus is Moon's exaltation sign; at time of activation Moon sits in Rohini nak which is Moon's OWN mulatrikona-adjacent nakshatra; this is the classical multi-layered Moon strengthening muhurta).
3. **Avoid direct confrontation with 11H-framing objectives** — chasing visible social-network "gain" targets against the 12H-delivery pattern works against the structure. Results arrive at 12H pathways, not 11H.

#### STR.01.C — Sun Integrity

**[L0 → L3]**

Sun is in Capricorn 21°57'35", nakshatra Shravana pada 4. Sun details:

| Dimension | Value |
|---|---|
| Rashi House | 10 (own Dig Bala territory — 10H is Sun's Dig Bala seat, contributing max 60 Dig Bala) |
| Chalit House | 11 |
| Shadbala | 8.51 Rupas (rank 1) |
| Shuddha Pinda | 172 (rank 2) |
| Vimsopaka | 11.6 (rank 3) |
| Avastha | Jaagrat / Kumar / Deena (awake / adolescent / humble) |
| Chara Karaka | Bhratrukaraka (BK) — siblings/guru/resources |
| Sthira Karaka | Atma (classical) — but operational Atma is Moon |

The Sun is the **strongest Shadbala planet** but his Avastha reads as "Deena" (humble). This is a paradox only superficially — the classical reading is that Sun-power is present (Shadbala) but Sun-expression is restrained (Deena). The Sun sits in Capricorn (Saturn's sign, neutral-to-inimical for Sun) which imports Saturnian restraint into his self-expression. Being Shravana pada 4 brings a Moon-ruled nakshatra on top of a Saturn-ruled sign — the ego-structure is layered with listening, receptivity, and operational restraint.

The **Sun Chalit shift +1 (10 → 11)** is operationally important:
- The Sun's RASHI position in 10H establishes him as directly angular (Dig Bala max 60).
- The Sun's CHALIT position in 11H delivers his outcome through gains, network, elder-influence channels.
- 5L Sun is a natural trikona lord; 5L in 11H (Chalit) is classical **Dhana Yoga** constituent (5L-11L connection by lord-in-house).

**Sun-Mercury conjunction in Capricorn**: Sun 21°57' and Mercury 00°50' — 21°07' apart; Mercury is within Sun's broader orbital proximity but NOT combust per v6.0 `[src: CMB.MERCURY]` (orb 14°). The wide Sun-Mercury coexistence in 10H forms **Budh-Aditya Yoga** (Sun-Mercury in same sign) — a classical communication-intelligence yoga. Its potency depends on Mercury not being combust; here Mercury is OUTSIDE combust range, so Budh-Aditya is fully formed and not debilitated.

#### STR.01.D — Atmakaraka consolidated view

The AK-Moon-in-D9-12H architecture produces a chart whose central purpose is NOT:
- Material accumulation for its own sake (2H is Bhavabala rank 11, weakest-but-one)
- Social prestige for its own sake (7H is weakest in Bhavabala, 12; AL in 10H provides public status as vehicle but not end)
- Family-lineage delivery (moon AK in 12H displaces this; Chandra Chart CHN shows house 2 = Pisces empty, house 12 = Cap has Sun+Mercury)

It IS:
- Dharma-delivery through 12H channels (foreign, dissolution, service, moksha)
- Wealth accumulated invisibly/asset-class/long-compounding rather than salary/income-bracket
- Public-career-as-platform (10H dense with AL, Sun, Mercury) for a 12H-delivered outcome

#### STR.01.E — Three-Interpretation Enumeration (AK-Moon D9-12H architecture)

Per §A.1 methodology: before committing to the primary interpretation, three competing readings are enumerated and weighed against the full evidence set.

```yaml
interpretation_A_foreign_income_architecture:
  claim: "AK-Moon in D9-12H + Chalit-12 delivery + Vargottama-Mercury-dispositor-from-Kendra = wealth accumulated via foreign/invisible/long-compounding channels, supported by visible 10H career platform."
  supporting_evidence:
    - D9.12H.DISP.VARG (YES) + D9.12H.DISP.PLACE (Kendra from D9 Lagna): Kendra-placement of a Vargottama dispositor converts what would otherwise be a pure-12H-dissolution into a structurally-grounded material channel. Kendra = material-foundation classical.
    - BVB.12 (rank 1, 506.09): The strongest house in the chart being 12th, with its lord Jupiter in own-sign-in-trikona (HSE.9), confirms 12H as OPERATIONAL-asset-house not debit-line.
    - PLN.SUN + PLN.MERCURY + ARD.AL all in 10H Capricorn: the visible-manifestation axis is densely populated, contradicting any pure-retreat reading.
    - CDL.MOON (12.21° drift from 11H cusp): Chalit-12 delivery is decisive, not borderline.
    - Current Mer MD + Sat AD both dispositors of the AK's delivery chains: the temporal architecture is maximally aligned.

interpretation_B_pure_moksha_sannyas:
  claim: "AK-in-D9-12H is classically a moksha / sannyas / renunciation indicator. The native's structural dharma is world-detachment, not material pursuit. Financial goal-setting works AGAINST chart-architecture."
  supporting_evidence:
    - Karakamsa in D9-12H (Karakamsa = AK-sign-in-D9 = Gemini, D9-12H): classical Jaimini label for this is 'moksha-karakamsa'.
    - AVS.MOON Susupta/Mrat/Shant: the AK is in 'dead/dormant/peaceful' Avastha, consistent with retreat rather than enterprise.
    - VIM Moon rank 7 LAST (9.1): the AK is Vimsopaka-weakest across vargas. A structurally-weak AK across vargas classically signals 'soul-burdened' rather than 'soul-empowered'.
    - BVB.7 rank 12 + BVB.2 rank 11: direct wealth/partnership houses are weakest — consistent with non-material chart.
    - SBL.TOTAL.VENUS below minimum (4.60 vs 5.50): Ishta-ruler is structurally weak, consistent with spiritual-intercession path over material-intercession path.

interpretation_C_foreign_residence_modest_material:
  claim: "Foreign residence IS central to dharma, AND material architecture exists, BUT the scale is modest-compound rather than 'immense'. The stated goal's 4 adjectives (immense/immediate/impeccable/irreversible) are architecturally unsupported at claimed magnitude."
  supporting_evidence:
    - AVG.SAV.PISCES (23) + AVG.SAV.AQUARIUS (23): the 11H and 12H bindu-support is chart-lowest. Even when these houses deliver, the bindu-floor damps amplitude.
    - CTR.01 Saturn Shuddha-Pinda rank 7 LAST: the chart's authority-planet has thin bindu-support, consistent with 'dramatic-inflection not cumulative-compound' delivery pattern. This argues against 'immense' scale outcomes and for sporadic-significant-events.
    - SIG.06 Sasha Yoga CYSS 79 (not 90+): mid-strength MPY, not peak.
    - YOG.SARA CYSS 91 (highest in chart): the chart's STRONGEST yoga is knowledge-pathway (Saraswati), NOT wealth-pathway (Lakshmi CYSS 77 is second-tier). Architectural emphasis is intellectual-scholarly over financial-commodity.
    - Venus MD is 2034+ (8 years out): the Ishta-ruler's full activation is distant; near-term material-Ishta-support is indirect only.

evidence_weighing:
  - A vs B: The D9-12H-stellium dispositor being KENDRA-PLACED + VARGOTTAMA is the decisive counter-evidence to pure-moksha reading. Pure-moksha configurations typically have weak dispositors or dispositors in Dusthana. Here the dispositor (Mercury) is in the 7th from D9 Lagna (Kendra) and is simultaneously the active MD lord. This structurally imports material-channel into the 12H-architecture. Reading B is ruled out.
  - A vs C: This is the GENUINE TENSION. A supports the architecture's existence; C calibrates its scale. Both can be simultaneously true: the architecture is real (A), but its scale is compound-over-decades rather than immediate-and-immense (C).
  - SIG.14 Sun Shadbala #1 with 10H position: the native possesses the raw positional-strength platform to host significant manifestation. Sun rank-1 at 10H is not a modest-outcome signature.
  - However, SBL.TOTAL.VENUS (4.60) + BVB.2 + BVB.7 all weak: the AMPLIFICATION pathway (Venus-mediated, 2H/7H-mediated) is weak. So the platform is strong, the amplifier is weak.

chosen_interpretation: "A as primary + C as scale-calibrator."
rationale: >
  The architecture exists and is unusually well-aligned temporally (A). The scale-expectation must
  be calibrated to compound-over-time rather than immediate-and-immense (C). The native's stated
  goal adjectives ('immense/immediate/impeccable/irreversible') are not directly supported at
  face value; what IS supported is 'structurally-well-architected long-compounding wealth with
  rare peak-inflection events during dasha-transit convergence windows'. This is a Saraswati-Yoga-
  inflected (knowledge/scholarship/foreign) path to wealth, not a Lakshmi-direct path.
  The 2027-01 to 2027-08 window is the primary near-term opportunity for peak-inflection; post-Ketu-MD
  (2027-08 onwards) the tempo shifts to transformation-oriented delivery.

interpretation_risk_B: >
  Low but nonzero. If the native's life trajectory over 2024-2027 has actually trended toward
  retreat/detachment despite material framing (e.g., chronic disengagement, repeated aborted
  material ventures, strong pull toward spiritual pursuits), then B may be closer to the truth
  than A+C. Self-observation over the current Mer-Sat AD provides the falsification test.

falsifier_for_chosen:
  - if_observed: "Mer-Sat AD window (2024-12 through 2027-08) closes with NO materially-channeled wealth accumulation despite high-DAS 36-month period, but significant life-reorientation toward service/retreat/inner-work"
    check_by: 2027-10-15
    implication: "B becomes primary; A+C framework is revised toward pure-moksha reading."
confidence_in_selection: 0.78
```

Mahalakshmi worship would need to be PRIMARY (not secondary to any other devata) to overcome the Venus-weakness."

Jupiter/Venus in 9H Sag = YES between (past Libra, approaching Ketu in Sco — wait, Sag is AFTER Sco going forward. So Jup/Ven are on the Ketu side not between Rahu-Ketu. Ketu=Sco, planet in Sag is 1 sign past Ketu). Check: Sun/Mercury in 10H Cap — 2 signs past Sco/Ketu. Moon in 11H Aqu — 3 signs past Ketu. These are on the KETU-side of the axis. For Kala Sarpa, ALL planets need to be on ONE side of the Rahu-Ketu axis. Here, Mars+Saturn sit on the Rahu→Ketu forward arc (Taurus-Gemini-Cancer-Leo-Virgo-Libra to Scorpio = yes forward); Jupiter/Venus/Sun/Mercury/Moon sit on the Ketu→Rahu forward arc (Scorpio onwards). Planets DO span BOTH arcs. FAILS Kala Sarpa strict test. Qualified Kala Amrita check also fails (need ALL planets within the Rahu-to-Ketu semicircle either direction).

Per §A.1: enumerate and weigh competing interpretations of the yoga inventory before selecting a primary reading.

```yaml

Financial outcomes arrive as COLLATERAL of intellectual/foreign/communication activity, not as primary-commercial pursuit."
  supporting_evidence:

evidence_weighing:
  - A vs B: B's dampers are real and non-trivial (Venus below min, Mercury below min, Sasha in weakest house). A's activation claim is structurally true at the dasha-timing level but faces operational dampers at the delivery level. Neither wins cleanly; they describe DIFFERENT layers of the same chart. A is correct about OPPORTUNITY; B is correct about CONVERSION-FRICTION.
  - A + B vs C: C introduces a PATHWAY dimension orthogonal to A/B. Even granting A (rich activation) and B (muted conversion), the QUESTION is: WHICH yoga converts most readily? The CYSS hierarchy answers: Saraswati. The native's financial outcome will most readily arrive via knowledge-mediated channels (analysis, teaching, writing, foreign-technical-consultancy, commentary, structured-advisory work) rather than via direct-commerce.
  - All three are partially correct; they operate at different analytical levels (A=temporal activation, B=conversion-friction, C=pathway-selection).

chosen_interpretation: "A + C combined, with B as an operational friction-factor to calibrate expectations."

  The chart HAS rich yoga activation (A), and that activation CHANNELS preferentially through
  knowledge/scholarship/intellectual-foreign pathways (C). B's dampers mean the magnitude of

  Mer-Sat AD window, with Lakshmi-direct pursuits (direct-commerce, family-2H-wealth,

  knowledge-mediated income acceleration despite running the maximum-Mercury activation window.

    check_by: 2027-08-21
```

### RPT.HSE.01 — House Axis 10-11-12 (Career/Gains/Foreign Architecture)

**[L0 → L6]**

This axis is the operational backbone of the chart's outward life. The three houses fold into one architecture because:
- 10H Capricorn holds AL (status-reflection) + Sun (ShadBala#1) + Mercury (MD lord, Vargottama)
- 11H Aquarius holds Moon (AK) in Rashi, PLUS Sun via Chalit (+1 drift)
- 12H Pisces has Bhavabala #1 (strongest house), lord Jupiter in own-sign 9H, and receives Chalit-Moon delivery
- The LORDS of 10 and 11 are BOTH Saturn (Capricorn 10H, Aquarius 11H both Saturn-ruled); 12H lord Jupiter sits in 9H in own sign

This means a SINGLE graha (Saturn) governs 10H+11H while another (Jupiter) governs 12H from the 9H — the three houses are controlled by only two planets, and those two planets have a mutual Dhana Yoga aspect.

#### HSE.01.A — House 10 (Capricorn) Forensic

```yaml
house: 10
sign: Capricorn
lord: Saturn
lord_placement: 7H Libra exalted, AmK, AD lord
rashi_occupants: [Sun (21°57' Shravana 4), Mercury (00°50' Uttara Ashadha 2)]
chalit_occupants: [Mercury] (Sun migrated to 11H chalit)
SAV: 26 (below chart-average 28.08)
bhavabala: 482.99 Virupa = 8.05 Rupas = rank 3 (strong)
bhavabala_components:
  lord_strength: 447.98 (Saturn)
  dig_bala: 60 (max — 10H is Sun's Dig Bala seat, Sat also gets nearly full)
  drik_bala: -24.99 (net negative aspectual load from Mars 4th + Saturn 10th to itself + Rahu 9th)
KP_significators: [Mercury, Venus, Mars, Ketu, Sun, Saturn]  # 6 planets — densely populated
KP_cusp_10_star_sub_subsub: [Sun, Saturn, Saturn]  # ALL three point to Sun/Saturn — the AD-lord axis
arudha: AL (Arudha Lagna)  # status-reflection lands here
sahams_landing: [Putra (Dhanishta)]
aspects_received_vedic: [Mars_4th (→Cap), Saturn_10th (self-aspect to natal 10H from 7H), Rahu_9th (→Cap)]
bhav_madhya_aspects_tight: [ASP.BM.SUN.10 (conj 0.56°), ASP.BM.JUPITER.10 (sext 1.15°), ASP.BM.NEPTUNE.10 (sext 2.62°), ASP.BM.PLUTO.10 (sext 1.82°)]
```

**[L2 interpretation]** Sun BhavMadhya conjunction at 0.56° means Sun is aligned within half-a-degree of the exact 10th-cusp-mid. Sun's raw potency is thus CONCENTRATED on the Midheaven delivery point. Mercury, though Rashi-positioned in 10H, is only 2.14° from the 10H-CUSP (early Capricorn) — so Mercury is at the *entry* of 10H while Sun is at its *peak*. This is a bi-strategic 10H staffing: Mercury represents the entry-path (trade, communication, early-career visibility) and Sun represents the peak-authority-delivery.

**[L3 convergence]** The KP cusp-10 chain (Sun→Saturn→Saturn) converges exactly with the Vimshottari Dasha lords currently running (Mer MD + Sat AD). KP sub-lord doctrine reads this as: the KP promise of 10H matters (career/status) is DUE during the current period. The KP system is the most event-timing-specific among the Vedic schools; this is a strong temporal signal.

**[L5 contradiction]** The 10H SAV is 26, BELOW the chart-average 28. Individual BAV contributions:
- Sun-BAV on Cap = 4 (average)
- Moon-BAV on Cap = 2 (WEAK — Moon is unsupportive of this sign)
- Mars-BAV on Cap = 3 (weak)
- Mercury-BAV on Cap = 5 (good)
- Jupiter-BAV on Cap = 6 (strong)
- Venus-BAV on Cap = 4 (average)
- Saturn-BAV on Cap = 2 (WEAK — Saturn himself gives only 2 bindus to his own 10th house)

The Saturn=2 on his OWN 10th is the key contradiction: Saturn *rules* the 10th but gives it minimum bindu-support. This is the Ashtakavarga equivalent of CTR.01 Saturn Shadbala-rank-2-vs-Shuddha-Pinda-rank-7 paradox. The 10H is loaded with AL + Sun + Mercury but its bindu floor is thin — meaning career WINS come in punctuated moments rather than compound accumulation, matching the Saturn-inflection reading.

#### HSE.01.B — House 11 (Aquarius) Forensic

```yaml
house: 11
sign: Aquarius
lord: Saturn (same as 10L)
rashi_occupants: [Moon (27°02' PB3)]
chalit_occupants: [Moon, + Sun (+1 chalit drift from 10H)]
SAV: 23 (LOW — among the three lowest)
bhavabala: 478.27 Virupa = 7.97 Rupas = rank 4 (strong)
bhavabala_components:
  lord_strength: 447.98 (Saturn)
  dig_bala: 40
  drik_bala: -9.71
KP_significators: [Sun, Rahu, Moon, Saturn]
KP_cusp_11_star_sub_subsub: [Mars, Mercury, Rahu]
arudhas_landing: [A7 (Partner Arudha)]
sahams_landing: [Karma (Aquarius, Dhanishta)]
bhav_madhya_aspects_tight: [ASP.BM.MOON.11 (conj 1.86°), ASP.BM.PLUTO.11 (sq 0.25°), ASP.BM.JUPITER.11 (sq 2.72°), ASP.BM.NEPTUNE.11 (sq 1.81°)]
```

**[L1 interpretation]** Moon conjuncts the 11H bhav-madhya within 1.86° — this is a tight alignment of Moon with the 11th-house delivery-point. But Moon's DEGREE is 27°02' and the 11H cusp is at Cap 19°32' — so Moon is 7.5° INTO the 11H's sign-span but 12.21° from the ASCENDING cusp of 11H AS MEASURED FROM THE DIRECTIONAL cusp (11H-cusp being Cap 19°32' going into Aqu 6°06' mid-bhava, Moon at Aqu 27°02' is WELL PAST the mid-bhava and 7°02' from the 12H cusp of Aqu 22°41'). So Moon's Chalit-12 classification (distance to NEAREST cusp is 11H cusp Aqu 6°06' — 12.21° back) is correct per v6.0; but Moon is simultaneously approaching the 12H cusp. Moon is transitional between 11H and 12H, but Sripathi places her at 12H due to nearer-to-12th-cusp geometry in the degree-based system.

**[L4 temporal stacking]** The 11H cusp star-sub-subsub chain (Mars, Mercury, Rahu) is a difficult signifier set for 11H gains:
- Mars (Lagna lord in 7H, enemy sign) — action-through-partnership
- Mercury (MD lord, Vargottama) — communication/trade
- Rahu (North Node) — unorthodox / foreign / ambition-driven gains

The Mercury-in-cusp-11-chain during Mercury MD is a temporal match. Rahu-transit axis currently in Aquarius (until Dec 5 2026) directly transits the 11H cusp — Rahu lands on its own nakshatra-lord-lane of KP.CUSP.11.

**[L5 contradiction]** The 11H has:
- SAV 23 (one of the three LOWEST signs, tied Pisces)
- Bhavabala rank 4 (strong)
- Saturn as lord (Shadbala #2, AD lord, Yogini lord from Dec 2026)

Bhavabala strong + SAV weak → classical "strong-but-unsupported" house. 11H gains arrive but require Saturn-scale effort to extract them (each bindu "missing" below SAV=28 = additional labor demand).

#### HSE.01.C — House 12 (Pisces) Forensic

```yaml
house: 12
sign: Pisces

bhav_madhya_aspects_tight: [ASP.BM.PLUTO.12.Q (quinc 0.22°), ASP.BM.PLUTO.12.T (trine 1.82°)]
```

**[L3 convergence]** The 12H convergence collapses into a tight triplet:
1. BVB rank 1 structural strength
2. Own-sign lord in trikona
3. Chalit-delivery of Moon-as-AK via the +1 drift
4. KP cusp chain matching AD lord Saturn

Combined with D9 12H stellium (three planets including the AK disposited by Vargottama Mercury from Kendra), this is a fourfold convergence on 12H across:
- D1 Rashi lord-dignity
- D1 Bhavabala composite
- D1 Chalit delivery
- D9 dharma-chart stellium

**[L6 intervention — 12H-specific]** The 12H delivery mechanism needs the following supports per classical Parashari prescription:
- **Jupiter-propitiation** through its own-sign-strength amplification (since Jupiter is 12L). Guru mantras, Yellow Sapphire is the classical gemstone for Jupiter but must be tested against the dasha-lord interference (Yellow Sapphire in Mercury MD creates functional friction — preferentially defer to Mercury MD-activator stones like Emerald first).
- **Mahalakshmi worship as Ishta Devata** aligns with the 12H-architecture because the classical derivation of Ishta from 12th-from-AK-in-D9 literally activates the 12H axis. This is the primary-pathway devata.
- **Foreign-income / invisible-asset channels** should be privileged over visible-network channels. This is not a spiritual claim — it is a structural reading: the Bhavabala-strongest house delivers, and the Bhavabala-weakest (7H/2H) under-delivers, so the ROUTING of effort matters.

#### HSE.01.D — 10-11-12 Axis synthesis

The 10H visibility (AL + Sun + Mercury) is the *vehicle*; the 11H/12H (esp. 12H via Chalit-Moon) is the *delivery channel*. A common misreading would treat 11H as the gain-source (Moon in 11H = classic "social network gains" signature); the Chalit-12 correction reverses this, placing gains through 12H channels. The 10H's role is to provide the *public-facing platform* on which 12H-channel income rides.

This structurally matches: career is built at work of long duration with quiet authority (Saturn 10L/11L in 7H), communication-trade is the instrument (Mercury in 10H, Vargottama, MD lord), and the wealth lives in 12H-signified territory (foreign, invisible-asset, large-investment, compounding, service).

#### HSE.01.E — Three-Interpretation Enumeration (10-11-12 axis character)

Per §A.1: the 10-11-12 axis admits at least three competing readings. Each is enumerated and weighed.

```yaml
interpretation_A_layered_delivery_vehicle_to_channel:
  claim: "10H (visible platform) → Chalit-11H Sun (gains delivery) → Chalit-12H Moon (foreign/invisible delivery). Career is the VEHICLE; 11H/12H are the CHANNELS. Income visibly tags 11H (gains) while actually accumulating in 12H (invisible-asset)."
  supporting_evidence:
    - CKS.SUN (+1 Chalit to 11H): Sun's outcome-delivery shifts to gains-house
    - CKS.MOON (+1 Chalit to 12H, 12.21° from 11H cusp): Moon's outcome-delivery shifts to foreign-house
    - ARD.AL in Capricorn 10H: public-image anchored in career-visibility
    - BVB.10 rank 3 + BVB.11 rank 4 + BVB.12 rank 1 — all three houses are Bhavabala-strong, supporting tri-house reading over single-house dominance
    - KP.CUSP.10 Star-Sub-SubSub (Sun/Saturn/Saturn) matches Mer-Sat AD
    - Memory-framework's "foreign-income architecture" derives from exactly this chain

interpretation_B_10H_primary_density:
  claim: "The 10H is the REAL signal. It houses AL + Sun + Mercury + has Bhavabala rank 3 + receives Mars 4th + Saturn 10th + Rahu 9th aspects. The Chalit shifts are degree-based refinements, not primary interpretive frame. This is a CAREER-CHART, period."
  supporting_evidence:
    - 10H tenant-density: 2 planets (Sun + Mercury) plus AL (Arudha point)
    - Sun Shadbala rank 1 in 10H = strongest planet in the career house
    - Mercury closest-to-cusp (2.14°) = cusp-lord in the career house
    - Triple-aspect convergence (Mars 4th, Saturn 10th, Rahu 9th)
    - D10 Saturn in 10H kendra + Leo D10 Lagna = D10 reinforces career as primary chart-axis
    - Sripathi-Chalit is one of several house systems; Rashi-placement is equally authoritative in BPHS tradition
    - A reader who rejects Chalit-priority doctrine arrives here

interpretation_C_12H_bhavabala_dominance:
  claim: "Bhavabala rank #1 (12H, 506.09 Virupa) is decisive. The chart's STRONGEST house is 12H. 10H/11H exist as VEHICLES to feed the 12H. The 'invisible wealth' reading: public career + network gains → 12H-asset-compounding. This is a 12H-chart dressed in 10H-clothing."
  supporting_evidence:
    - BVB.12 rank 1 (506.09) vs BVB.10 rank 3 (482.99) vs BVB.11 rank 4 (478.27): 12H is BhavaBALA-STRONGEST
    - 12L Jupiter in own sign in 9H trikona (lord-in-own-in-trikona = Bhavat-Bhavam intensification)
    - D9 12H Gemini stellium (Moon+Jupiter+Rahu) — D9-level reinforcement of 12H-as-architectural-spine
    - Karakamsa (AK in D9) in D9-12H Gemini — dharma-chart places soul-purpose in 12H
    - Moon AK in Chalit-12 delivery
    - Four independent convergences on 12H (Bhavabala, Bhavat Bhavam, D9 stellium, Karakamsa, Chalit-Moon) — the densest single-house convergence in the chart
    - Classical signature: when 12H is strongest, WEALTH LIVES THERE (invisible asset-class, foreign holdings, long-compounding portfolios, moksha-adjacent accumulation)

evidence_weighing:
  - A is the SYNTHESIS reading that integrates B's 10H-density with C's 12H-Bhavabala-dominance, using Chalit as the mechanical bridge between them
  - B is correct that 10H is densely occupied — but ignores the Bhavabala hierarchy (BVB.12 > BVB.10) and the Chalit degree-geometry
  - C is correct that 12H dominates by Bhavabala — but ignores that 12H has NO TENANTS in Rashi (only a Chalit-drift Moon), meaning 12H's dominance is STRUCTURAL (lord + aspects + D9 reinforcement) not POPULATED
  - The Chalit degree-geometry (CKS.SUN +1, CKS.MOON +1) is the mechanical link: it converts a 10H-populated-density into an 11H/12H-delivery-pattern. Without Chalit-priority, B wins; with Chalit-priority, A wins. With Bhavabala-primacy, C wins.
  - The three readings resolve ordinally: C (structure) > A (mechanism) > B (visible)

chosen_interpretation: "A (layered delivery) as operational reading, with C (12H-structural-dominance) as architectural foundation."
rationale: >
  The chart's STRUCTURAL priority (C) is that 12H dominates. The chart's OPERATIONAL mechanism (A) is
  that 10H/11H visibility feeds 12H delivery via Chalit shifts. B is a reader-choice that rejects
  the Chalit-priority doctrine; within this report's v6.0-declared §0 rule ('Chalit primary for
  transit-trigger and outcome delivery'), A+C is the correct composite reading.
  Operational implication: the native should structure career/visibility (10H) and networking (11H)
  as INSTRUMENTS for 12H-channel accumulation, NOT as ends in themselves. Foreign exposure,
  invisible-asset building (holdings outside immediate view), long-compounding investments, and
  service-infrastructure are the actual wealth-vehicles. Income visible in a salary/fee channel
  is the 10H/11H appearance; the accumulation happens in 12H-signified territory.

interpretation_risk_B_dominance: >
  If the native's operational style strongly rejects Chalit-priority (e.g., treats everything as
  Rashi-primary), then B becomes the effective working frame and wealth is read as direct-10H-career-
  income. Outcomes would be constrained to what the 10H + 11H can directly produce, not what the
  12H can compound.

  - if_observed: "Material accumulation over 2026-2028 shows up almost entirely in directly-visible/liquid channels (bank balances, salary, immediate fees) with no growth in 12H-signified channels (foreign holdings, long-horizon investments, invisible-compounding)"
    check_by: 2028-08-21
    implication: "C is wrong about 12H operational dominance; re-read as B with A as secondary flavor."
confidence_in_selection: 0.82
```

### RPT.HSE.02 — House 2 and House 7 Weakness (The Structural Fragile Zones)

**[L0 → L5]**

Bhavabala rank 11 (2H) and rank 12 (7H) are the two WEAKEST houses in the chart. Both are Venus-ruled. Both share the Bhavabala-weakness with a Venus-Shadbala-weakness at the lord level. This is a triple-weakness stack on the Venus-axis that deserves explicit treatment.

#### HSE.02.A — House 2 (Taurus — Family/Savings/Speech)

```yaml
house: 2
sign: Taurus
lord: Venus
lord_placement: 9H Sagittarius (Jupiter's sign, friendly-to-Venus, exaltation deg Pisces 27° not applicable here)
rashi_occupants: [Rahu (19°01' Rohini 3)]
chalit_occupants: [Rahu]
SAV: 29 (chart-average)
bhavabala: 266.26 Virupa = 4.44 Rupas = rank 11 (second-weakest)
KP_significators: [Rahu, Venus]  # sparse
KP_cusp_2_star_sub_subsub: [Moon, Rahu, Saturn]
arudhas_landing: [A6 (Enemy Arudha)]
sahams_landing: [Punya (Rohini)]
```

**[L2]** Rahu in 2H Taurus Rohini is a classical "sudden-rise wealth via unconventional means" marker in Parashari tradition. Rohini is Moon's own nakshatra (ruled by Moon the exalted lord of Taurus), making Rahu-in-Rohini a particularly potent placement — Rahu takes on some of Moon's fertility/attraction quality, amplified by Rahu's taste-for-material of 2H. The risk: Rahu-2H is also a classical "family turbulence / speech disputes / unsteady wealth cycles" indicator.

**[L3]** A6 (enemy Arudha) in 2H is a structural stress point — opposition/rivalry manifests in the wealth domain. Combined with Venus-as-2L being the weakest Shadbala planet, 2H direct-wealth-accumulation is under-supported. The chart is not built for family-inheritance wealth or traditional asset-family accumulation. It IS built for 12H invisible-channel accumulation per HSE.01.

**[L4 temporal]** Rahu's transit through Capricorn (Dec 5 2026 — June 2028) casts its 9th aspect on Taurus (natal 2H, its own natal position)! This is a RAHU RETURN in aspect — a classical 18-year event activating 2H natal signatures. Starts Dec 5 2026 when Rahu enters Capricorn.

#### HSE.02.B — House 7 (Libra — Partnership/Spouse/Counterparts)

```yaml
house: 7
sign: Libra
lord: Venus (same as 2L)
lord_placement: 9H Sagittarius
rashi_occupants: [Saturn (22°27' Vishakha 1), Mars (18°31' Swati 4)]
chalit_occupants: [Saturn, Mars]
SAV: 33 (among chart HIGHEST, tied Scorpio)
bhavabala: 253.36 Virupa = 4.22 Rupas = rank 12 (WEAKEST house)
KP_significators: [Moon, Saturn, Venus]
KP_cusp_7_star_sub_subsub: [Rahu, Saturn, Jupiter]
bhrigu_bindu_lands_here: YES (8°04' Libra in Swati 1)
varshphal_muntha_current: Libra 7H (2026-02-05 → 2027-02-05)
sahams_landing: []
aspects_received: Mars (4/7/8), Saturn (3/7/10), Jupiter (5/7/9) — all special aspects
```

**[L5 contradiction]** The 7H paradox:
- SAV 33 (one of the chart HIGHEST — strong bindu-support)
- Bhavabala 4.22 Rupas (rank 12 — WEAKEST house)
- Contains Sasha Yoga (Saturn exalted in 7 kendra)
- Contains Lagna-lord Mars
- Venus 7L is Shadbala rank 7 (weakest planet)
- Receives all three special-aspect-type planets (Mars 7th, Saturn 7th, Jupiter 5th/7th/9th does not land on 7H — Jupiter from Sag casts 5th on Aries, 7th on Gemini, 9th on Leo — NOT on Libra 7H)

Wait — correction: Jupiter from Sagittarius 9H: 5th aspect = Aries 1H, 7th aspect = Gemini 3H, 9th aspect = Leo 5H. Jupiter does NOT aspect 7H Libra natally. The 7H is thus OUTSIDE Jupiter's natal protective aspect range. This is important — the 7H is UNBLESSED by Jupiter's natal aspect, unusual for a house that carries Sasha Yoga.

The 7H Bhavabala rank 12 reconciles with the Saturn-Shadbala-2-vs-Shuddha-Pinda-7 pattern (CTR.01): Saturn's dramatic-inflection pattern applies at the house level too. The 7H is the CHART'S MOST INFLECTION-PRONE POINT — maximum-dignity planet in minimum-Bhavabala house. The Bhrigu Bindu (destiny focal point) lands here. The Varshphal Muntha lands here for the current year. The partnership domain is where the chart's high-leverage crises AND high-leverage breakthroughs concentrate.

**[L6]** 7H interventions need to address TWO things simultaneously:
1. Strengthen Venus (7L) — via appropriate Venus gemstone (Diamond/White Sapphire) but NOT during active Mercury-MD period since Venus is enemy of the dasha lord (Mercury) and also during Venus MD (2034+) Platinum should be used
2. Moderate Mars-Saturn conjunction tension in 7H — traditional prescription: Hanuman (Mars-pacification, Chalisa/44) + Shani (Saturn-pacification, Kala Bhairava or Hanuman as Shani-appeaser depending on tradition)

Mars-Saturn-conjunction 7.38° orb is classical "career-stress-and-partnership-friction" signature. Not extinguished by Sasha Yoga (which is Saturn-strengthening, not Mars-pacifying).

#### HSE.02.C — Venus axis synthesis

Venus is:
- 2L + 7L (two weakest Bhavabala houses)
- Ishta Devata ruler (Mahalakshmi) — see RPT.DEV.01
- Shadbala rank 7 (weakest)
- Shuddha Pinda rank 5 (middle)
- Vimsopaka rank 6 (9.5)
- In 9H trikona (dignity-wise decent)
- Conjunct Neptune 1.81° (tight Western) + conjunct Jupiter 3.76° + sextile Mars 2.68°

The Venus-weakness does NOT destroy the yogas Venus participates in (Saraswati, Lakshmi, both NBRYs involve Venus). It MODULATES the delivery: Venus-mediated outcomes (partnerships, creative-wealth, 7H/2H rulership outcomes) arrive slower and require more effort. Venus-intercession (Mahalakshmi) remains the prescribed Ishta path despite the weakness — classical doctrine holds that weak Ishta rulers REQUIRE more direct worship, not less, and that the devata operates through the ruler rather than being limited by it.

#### HSE.02.D — Three-Interpretation Enumeration (Venus-axis weakness)

Per §A.1: the 2H/7H weakness and Venus-axis pattern admits competing readings.

```yaml
interpretation_A_venus_axis_fragile_compensated_by_12H:
  claim: "2H/7H/Venus is a genuine structural weakness triad (Bhavabala ranks 11, 12; Venus Shadbala below min). The chart COMPENSATES architecturally by routing wealth through 12H (Chalit-Moon delivery, D9 stellium, Bhavabala #1) rather than through direct 2H/7H channels. Weakness is real but NOT disabling — it's redirected."
  supporting_evidence:
    - BVB.2 rank 11 (4.44 Rupas) + BVB.7 rank 12 (4.22 Rupas): both Venus-ruled houses are weakest pair
    - SBL.TOTAL.VENUS 4.60 (below min 5.50): lord-level weakness confirmed
    - BVB.12 rank 1 (8.43 Rupas) compensates by providing an ALTERNATIVE wealth-channel
    - Chalit-12H Moon delivers via the strongest-Bhavabala house
    - Jupiter 12L in own sign 9H provides 12H-lord-strength in lieu of Venus 2L/7L strength
    - Memory-framework's foreign-income architecture is precisely this compensation structure

interpretation_B_venus_axis_weakness_dominates:
  claim: "Venus weakness is not 'compensated'; it's a real ceiling on partnership, creative-wealth, and direct-accumulation outcomes. The 12H compensation works for SOME wealth forms but cannot substitute for partnership/relationship/family-wealth, which require 2H/7H to be functional. The native's relationship/partnership axis is a life-long fragility, NOT an architectural redirection."
  supporting_evidence:
    - Bhrigu Bindu (destiny-focus) lands in Libra 7H (8°04' Swati 1) — destiny concentrates AT the fragile axis
    - Varshphal Muntha 2026-02-05 to 2027-02-05 in Libra 7H — current-year focus compounds on fragile axis
    - Mars + exalted-Saturn conjunction in 7H (orb 7.38°) — Mars-Saturn karmic-friction signature at the partnership locus
    - Jupiter does NOT aspect 7H natally (Sag 9th's 5/7/9 aspects miss Libra) — 7H is unblessed by natal Jupiter
    - A2 lands in 2H + A6 (enemy Arudha) in 2H — competition/enmity in the wealth-image axis
    - Venus as Ishta-ruler weakness means the SPIRITUAL intercession channel itself carries karmic burden
    - Reading: the native's relationship/partnership/direct-wealth outcomes will carry friction even during peak-timing windows

interpretation_C_split_signification_planet_vs_house:
  claim: "The 7H holds Sasha Yoga (CYSS 79) with exalted Saturn, yet 7H is Bhavabala-weakest. This is NOT a contradiction to resolve; it's a BIMODAL reading. The 7H produces strong-Saturn-PLANETARY outcomes (authority, career-partners, external-discipline-figures) while simultaneously producing weak-HOUSE-SUBSTANCE outcomes (spouse-specific, private-partnership, relationship-intimacy). Reading the 7H as 'weak' is wrong; reading it as 'strong' is also wrong."
  supporting_evidence:
    - YOG.SASHA CYSS 79 + PLN.SATURN exalted: strong planetary signature
    - BVB.7 rank 12: weak house-substance signature
    - SIG.12 Mars Shuddha Pinda #1 in 7H: yet another planet performs strongly in the 7H
    - CVG.08 Aries-Libra axis triple-aspect convergence (Mars 7th, Saturn 7th, Jupiter 5th to Aries Lagna): the AXIS is active even as the HOUSE-substance is weak
    - Classical precedent: Mahapurusha Yoga in a weak Bhavabala house produces 'public-authority without private-intimacy' pattern (Saravali)

evidence_weighing:
  - A + C vs B: A and C describe DIFFERENT layers of the same chart. A is the architectural compensation (chart routes wealth to 12H). C is the split-signification at the specific 7H (strong-planet in weak-house = public-authority not private-intimacy). B is the unmitigated-weakness reading, which under-weights the 12H compensation.
  - A partially overlaps with B: A acknowledges Venus-weakness is REAL; A differs from B in claiming REDIRECTION rather than CEILING. The evidence for redirection is the 12H Bhavabala dominance + D9 stellium + Chalit-Moon delivery — all real, all structurally present.
  - C is the 7H-specific refinement. It explains WHY the chart simultaneously has Sasha and the weakest Bhavabala in the same house.
  - B is not rulable-out: the 12H compensation works for compounding-wealth but NOT for relationship-intimacy or family-inheritance channels. If the native prioritizes relationship-fulfillment or 2H-family-wealth as primary outcomes, B is closer to the operative truth.

chosen_interpretation: "A (redirected compensation) + C (split signification at 7H). B treated as falsifier-trigger for relationship-specific outcomes."
rationale: >
  The chart redirects wealth-channels from 2H/7H (weak) to 12H (strong) at the architectural level.
  Within the 7H specifically, strong-PLANET + weak-HOUSE produces public-authority-role-outcomes
  (career partners, external adversaries, structural-discipline-counterparts) without equivalent
  private-intimacy outcomes. Venus-Ishta weakness is compensated in wealth-axis but not in
  Venus-specific-signification-axis (creative-expression, relationship-intimacy, personal-aesthetic).
  Operational implication: the native should NOT expect 2H/7H to deliver relationship-or-family-wealth
  at the same standard as the 12H compounds. The Mahalakshmi worship path is PRIMARY for wealth
  intercession but does NOT automatically also heal the 2H/7H signification domains — those require
  separate attention if they are life-priorities.

interpretation_risk_B_dominance: >
  If relationship/partnership/family-wealth is central to the native's lived-experience objective
  (not stated in the framework but possibly implicit), then B's fragility-reading dominates and the
  chart's compensation is insufficient. This is a scope-issue: the report addresses FINANCIAL goal
  (memory-framework), not relationship/family goals.

falsifier_for_chosen:
  - if_observed: "Partnership or family-wealth domains show sustained crisis (not just friction) during 2026-2029 despite 12H-compensation architecture being active"
    check_by: 2029-04-16
    implication: "B's ceiling-reading is correct; the 12H compensation is domain-specific to financial-accumulation, not to Venus-signification-domains."
  - if_observed: "2H and 7H transit-triggered events (Rahu-Cap Dec 5 2026 onward; Saturn's 7th aspect returns during Aries transit) deliver STRONGLY rather than weakly, contradicting Bhavabala rank 11/12 framing"
    check_by: 2028-06-30
    implication: "SAV 29/33 (adequate) may matter more than Bhavabala rank for transit-triggered delivery; HSE.02 weakness framing requires calibration to transit vs natal contexts."
confidence_in_selection: 0.76
```

### RPT.DVS.01 — D10 Dashamsha Career Architecture

**[L0 → L4]**

D10 Lagna is Leo. Leo-D10-Lagna is ruled by Sun, who in D1 is the Shadbala rank-1 planet and occupies 10H Capricorn. Sun's strong D1 position provides dignity to D10-Lagna.

```yaml
D10_Lagna_sign: Leo (ruler Sun D1-rank-1)
D10_placements:
  - D10.SUN: Aries (D10 9H) — own trikona, fiery, lord of D10 Lagna in 9H-from-D10-Lagna
  - D10.MOON: Scorpio (D10 4H) — DEBILITATION
  - D10.MARS: Aries (D10 9H) — own sign, Mars in Sun's trikona = Raja Yoga material
  - D10.MERCURY: Virgo (D10 2H) — own sign, earning / wealth house
  - D10.JUPITER: Pisces (D10 8H) — own sign BUT in Dusthana — transformational-career signature
  - D10.VENUS: Gemini (D10 11H) — mental-commerce house
  - D10.SATURN: Taurus (D10 10H) — ANGULAR, in an earth sign, AMK karaka in 10H of D10
  - D10.RAHU: Cancer (D10 12H)
  - D10.KETU: Capricorn (D10 6H)
```

Key readings:

**[L2]** Saturn in D10 10H — this is THE career-architectural fact. Saturn as AmK (Amatyakaraka, the career-karaka in Jaimini) sitting in the 10th house of the D10 career chart is a DOUBLE activation of Saturn's career-role. The sign is Taurus (Venus-ruled, friendly-to-Saturn in Parashari) — Saturn is steady, earth-bound, asset-building in the career domain. Combined with D1 Saturn exalted in 7H, the career-axis Saturn is fourfold-reinforced: D1-exalt + AmK + D10-10H + exalt-near-max.

**[L2]** Sun in D10 9H Aries + Mars in D10 9H Aries — two fiery planets in the D10 9th (dharma-of-career). Mars is in his OWN sign in 9th = confers technical-mastery signature; Sun as D10-Lagna lord placed in 9th-from-self establishes dharmic-career orientation (work is pursued as a dharma, not only transactionally).

**[L3]** D10-Lagna-lord Sun in D10 9H + AmK Saturn in D10 10H + D1-MD-lord Mercury in D10 2H own sign forms a **triangulated career architecture**:
- 2H (D10): Mercury (D1 MD lord) — earning/income
- 9H (D10): Sun (D10 Lagna lord) — dharma/direction
- 10H (D10): Saturn (AmK, D1 AD lord) — execution/status

All three trikonal/kendra positions filled by currently-active Vimshottari lords (Mer MD + Sat AD) or by chart-pillar planets (Sun Shadbala #1). This is a current-dasha-activates-D10-career structure.

**[L5]** The Moon debilitated in D10 4H is a red flag: emotional-home-stability-during-career is compromised. The D10 Moon debilitation is NOT cancelled (Moon's dispositor in D10 is Mars-in-Aries — Aries is NOT a kendra from D10-Lagna Leo; 9th is a trikona, not a kendra). So Moon's D10 debility stands. Classical reading: career-pursuit is likely to be pursued at cost of emotional-home or requires physical dislocation from home of origin — aligning with the 12H foreign-income architecture.

**[L6]** D10 interventions are specifically Saturn-strengthening (the D10 10L + AmK) and Mercury-MD-aligned. Precisely the current memory-framework protocol. The D10 validates the protocol architecture.

The Moon's D60 label "Krura" (harsh) adds to the AK-is-subtly-burdened reading. The Saturn D60 label "Saumya" (peaceful) reinforces Saturn-as-karmic-ally despite the Shadbala-vs-Shuddha-Pinda tension. The Sun label "Amrita" (nectar) re-emphasizes Sun as positive past-karma — aligning with Ketu-Sun sub-period 2028-07 to 2029-03 as a "past-karma-nectar-harvest" window within Ketu MD.

#### DVS.02.B — [L4 temporal stacking] + [L5 contradiction check]

**[L4 temporal stacking]** The D60 deity-labels interact with the 36-month Vimshottari/transit window as follows:

- **Ketu MD opens 2027-08-21** with Ketu in D60 Capricorn (8H of D60 from Leo D60 Lagna) — a Dusthana reinforcement. - **Saturn AD (current, through 2027-08-21)** carries D60 "Saumya" (peaceful) signature for Saturn. This softens the severity of the Saturn Shuddha-Pinda-weakness from CTR.01 — past-karma treats Saturn as a benevolent karmic ally. The Ketu-MD opening then HANDS OFF to a Ketu whose D60 placement is NOT softened.
- **Ketu-Sun sub-period 2028-07-24 → 2029-03-18** activates Sun's D60 "Amrita" (nectar) label during a natal-Sun-eclipse window (TLE Aug 6 2028 per TRN.03). The D60 Amrita reinforces the eclipse as a KARMIC-NECTAR opening rather than a destructive hit — the eclipse activates positive past-karma.

**[L5 contradiction check]** A potential contradiction: if D60 Moon is "Krura" (harsh) and Moon is AK, then the soul-level past-karma carries harsh residues — which tensions against the chart's foreign-income-architecture optimistic framing. Resolution: the Krura-Moon-AK past-karma explains the Avastha (Susupta/Mrat/Shant — dormant/dead/peaceful) — the Moon's dormancy in this life is itself the settlement of harsh past-karma. The present life's Moon-AK pathway is about ACCEPTING the dormancy/depth (12H Chalit, D9 12H) rather than forcing 11H-social-expansion. Material outcomes arrive BECAUSE the Moon consents to remain deep, not despite it.

### RPT.DSH.01 — Triple-Dasha Engine: Current Mercury MD — Saturn AD Window (through 2027-08-21)

**[L0 → L6]**

This is the highest-leverage 17-month window in the chart over the next 36 months per the D.5 heatmap. It combines:

- **Vimshottari** Mercury MD (2010-08-21 → 2027-08-21) + Saturn AD (2024-12-12 → 2027-08-21)
- **Yogini**: Bhadrika (Mercury) active through 2026-12-22, then Ulka (Saturn) through 2032-12-22
- **Jaimini Chara**: Scorpio MD (2026-02-05 → ~2035) + Libra AD (through 2027-01-05), then Virgo AD (2027-01-05 → 2027-12-05)

The overlap pattern over the 17 months:

| Month | Vim | Yogini | Chara | Same-Lord-Convergence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-04 to 2026-12 | Mer-Sat | Bhadrika (Mer) | Sco-Lib | Mer appears in Vim-MD AND Yog-MD (DOUBLE MERCURY); Sat is only in Vim-AD |
| 2026-12-22 to 2027-01-05 | Mer-Sat | Ulka (Sat) | Sco-Lib | Sat in Vim-AD AND Yog-MD (DOUBLE SATURN for 2 weeks) |
| 2027-01-05 to 2027-08-21 | Mer-Sat | Ulka (Sat) | Sco-Vir | Sat in Vim-AD AND Yog-MD (DOUBLE SATURN persisting) |

**The double-Mercury window** (through 2026-12-21, roughly 8 months) is when Mercury's effects are AMPLIFIED by appearing in two simultaneous dashas. Mercury's themes: communication, trade, short-travel, intellect, commerce, commissions, publication.

**The double-Saturn window** (starts 2026-12-22, persists through 2027-08-21 = 8 months) is when Saturn's effects are AMPLIFIED by Vimshottari-AD + Yogini-MD. Saturn's themes: authority, structure, long-term commitments, real estate, discipline-payoff, career-culmination.

**Chara shift to Scorpio-Virgo** (2027-01-05) introduces Virgo as an AD theme. Virgo is Mercury-ruled + Mercury's exaltation sign. A Virgo-AD during a Mercury MD is a Mercury-upon-Mercury magnification, precisely at the time Yogini-Mercury is ending. This creates a HANDOFF: Mercury-amplification via Yogini ends Dec 22, Mercury-amplification via Chara AD begins Jan 5. The 2-week gap is filled by Scorpio-Libra Chara AD where Libra = Venus sign = ties to 7H Sasha Yoga Saturn.

#### DSH.01.A — Dasha-Level Activation of Yogas

- **Saraswati Yoga** (CYSS 91) — Mer MD + Sat AD is maximum activation for Saraswati's Mercury member. Jupiter exaltation transit 2026-06 to 2026-10 adds Jupiter activation. Venus AD in Ketu MD (2028-01-18 → 2029-03-18) will add Venus activation later.
- **Sasha Yoga** (CYSS 79) — Sat AD is the MAXIMUM activation available in current century (next Sat MD is 2047). Sasha delivery is concentrated in this 17-month window.
- **Lakshmi Yoga** (CYSS 77) — partially activated by transit Jupiter exaltation. Full Vimshottari activation is Venus AD in Ketu MD.
- **Anapha Yoga** (CYSS 73) — fully activated throughout Mercury MD.
- **NBRY.SATURN** (CYSS 75) — activated by Saturn AD now.
- **NBRY.VENUS** (CYSS 70) — partially activated by Mercury MD (since Mercury is the cancellation agent); fully activated later in Venus AD.
- **Budh-Aditya** (CYSS 67) — activated through Mercury MD.
- **Dhana Saturn-Jupiter** (CYSS 56) — activated by Saturn AD.

**Total yoga-CYSS activated by this window**: sum of activated CYSS values with overlap-compensation ≈ 450+ (the DENSEST yoga-activation window available in the full Vimshottari sequence 2026-2060).

#### DSH.01.B — Sub-period (Pratyantardasha) Forward-model within Mer-Sat AD

The Vimshottari sub-period within Mercury-Saturn spans 2024-12-12 to 2027-08-21 (32 months). Sub-periods (Pratyantar dashas) within this AD follow the standard Vimshottari nested formula. Key estimated Mer-Sat-PD sub-periods (derived, not from v6.0 which only tracks to AD level):

| Sub-period (PD lord) | Approx duration | Approx dates |
|---|---|---|
| Mer-Sat-Sat | ~5.1 months | 2024-12-12 → 2025-05-18 |
| Mer-Sat-Mer | ~4.6 months | 2025-05-18 → 2025-10-03 |
| Mer-Sat-Ket | ~1.8 months | 2025-10-03 → 2025-11-28 |
| Mer-Sat-Ven | ~5.4 months | 2025-11-28 → 2026-05-16 |
| Mer-Sat-Sun | ~1.6 months | 2026-05-16 → 2026-07-06 |
| Mer-Sat-Moo | ~2.7 months | 2026-07-06 → 2026-09-29 |

| Mer-Sat-Jup | ~4.3 months | 2027-04-22 → 2027-08-21 |

These are approximate; exact boundaries should be recomputed against Vimshottari proportional formulas. The critical PD windows:
- **Mer-Sat-Moon** (2026-07 to 2026-09): PD lord is Moon = AK, so AK-activation via PD inside the densest window. Coincides with Jupiter exaltation transit and eclipse season (Aug 12 + Aug 28 eclipses).
- **Mer-Sat-Rahu** (2026-11 to 2027-04): Rahu's PD activation coincides with nodal axis shift Dec 5 and Yogini Bhadrika → Ulka transition.
- **Mer-Sat-Jupiter** (2027-04 to 2027-08): Jupiter PD within Saraswati's maximum activation window AND coincides with Jupiter's second exaltation pass in Cancer (2027-04 direct in Cancer).

```yaml

Expecting 'immense financial harvest' from this window may under-deliver even as 'substantial knowledge-platform construction' over-delivers."

evidence_weighing:
  - A vs B: A treats current window as PEAK; B treats it as PLANTING. The truth is empirically resolvable only retrospectively. The dasha-classical literature supports BOTH readings: Mer-Sat is classically described as 'consolidation under discipline' (B) AND 'Saturnine-testing-of-Mercury-gains' (A). B is the MORE conservative reading; A is the MORE goal-aligned reading.

rationale: >
  The current Mer-Sat AD is structurally the densest activation window available before 2047.
  Its OUTCOMES channel preferentially through Saraswati-aligned domains (knowledge work, foreign
  intellectual exposure, technical-advisory, analytical publication, communication-density).

  Treat direct-commerce pipelines as SUPPORTIVE during this window; build the primary commerce

  (2028-01+) when Venus activates directly.

  (dramatic-inflection-not-compound-gains), then Mer-Sat AD under-delivers at compound scale and
```

### RPT.DSH.02 — Ketu Mahadasha (2027-08-21 → 2034-08-21) — Regime Change

**[L0 → L5]**

Ketu MD is a 7-year window. Ketu occupies Scorpio 8H (19°01' Jyeshtha 1). 8H is a Dusthana; Scorpio is ruled by Mars (Shuddha Pinda rank 1, Lagna lord). Jyeshtha is ruled by Mercury (the OUTGOING MD lord). This creates a Mercury-to-Ketu transition through Mercury's own nakshatra — a structurally-smoothed handoff.

```yaml
Ketu_D1: Scorpio 19°01' Jyeshtha pada 1
Ketu_Rashi_house: 8
Ketu_Chalit_house: 8 (no shift)
Ketu_dispositor: Mars (Libra 7H)
Ketu_nakshatra_ruler: Mercury (outgoing MD)
Ketu_D9: Sagittarius (ruled Jupiter, 12H of D9 = Gemini's opposite = 6th from D9 Lagna Cancer — different house-position than D9 12H stellium)
Wait — 6th from Cancer = Sagittarius. So D9 Ketu is in D9 6H.
So D9.KETU = Sagittarius = D9 6H (Cancer-based)
Ketu_in_D10: Capricorn D10 6H — Dusthana reinforcement
```

**[L2]** Ketu in 8H Scorpio is a CLASSIC "moksha / occult / transformation / inheritance / research" signature. Jyeshtha pada 1 is a fierce nakshatra pada linked to leadership through struggle.

**[L3]** Ketu's tight Western aspects (v6.0 §16.2): 
- Mercury-Ketu QUINCUNX 0.50° — TIGHTEST aspect in whole chart; entire Mercury MD carried this quincunx
- Venus-Ketu SEXTILE 1.53°
- Moon-Ketu CONJUNCTION 9.89°
- Uranus-Ketu CONJUNCTION 9.89°

Ketu's strongest contact in the chart is Mercury (quincunx). The 0.50° Mercury-Ketu tension has been running throughout Mercury MD; it's the BACKGROUND cosmic aperture the outgoing MD operated through. In Ketu MD, Ketu activates ITS own themes without Mercury-mediation — the quincunx-tension relaxes because Mercury is no longer the primary actor.

**[L4]** Ketu MD sub-periods first two years:
- Ketu-Ketu: 2027-08-21 → 2028-01-18 (~5 months)
- Ketu-Venus: 2028-01-18 → 2029-03-18 (~14 months) — **Venus AD activates NBRY-Venus, Ishta-Devata-ruler, Lakshmi Yoga Venus**
- Ketu-Sun: 2029-03-18 → 2029-07-24 (~4 months) — **Sun AD activates NBRY-Saturn** (Sun is the cancellation agent)
- Ketu-Moon: 2029-07-24 → 2030-02-24 (~7 months) — **AK activation within Ketu MD**

The Ketu-Venus sub-period is the **NBRY-Venus delivery peak** AND the Ishta-Devata-direct-ruler dasha. This is a specifically-calibrated spiritual-wealth window per classical doctrine.

The Ketu-Sun sub-period activates the OTHER NBRY (Saturn via Sun). Together Ketu-Venus + Ketu-Sun = 18 months of sequential NBRY activations.

**[L5]** Ketu MDs are classically called "Moksha-delivering" but also "sudden-change-producing" periods. The theme of the MD depends on Ketu's placement. Here, 8H-Scorpio-Jyeshtha-quincunx-Mercury indicates:
- Research, investigation, occult-study, hidden-asset-work
- Reputation-shifts from Mercury-MD's visible-path to Ketu-MD's hidden-path
- Potential for large transformational events (8H) that redefine the life-structure

The Ketu MD is DIFFERENT from the Mercury MD in character. Mer MD was 17 years of steady, communication-and-commerce-channeled, visible-platform-building. Ketu MD is 7 years of transformation, hidden-channels, spiritual-discovery, and sudden-redirection.

### RPT.TRN.01 — Saturn Transit Engine (36-month horizon)

**[L0 → L4]**

Saturn's 36-month path through Pisces and Aries (per search-verified Lahiri ephemeris, retrieved 2026-04-16):

```yaml
saturn_transit_path:
  2025-03-30 → 2026-03-29: Pisces direct+retro
  2026-03-29 → 2026-07-26: Aries 0°–7° direct (CURRENT as of 2026-04-16)
  2026-07-27 → 2026-09(late): Aries retrograde, back to ~Pisces
  2026-09(late) → 2026-12-11: Pisces retrograde, SD at ~Pis 22°-24°
  2026-12-11 → 2027-04(mid): Pisces direct
  2027-04(mid) → 2027-08-09: Aries direct 0°–27°
  2027-08-09 → 2027-12-24: Aries retrograde, back toward Pisces per Lahiri
  2027-10-20 → 2028-02-23: Pisces retrograde (re-entry per v6.0 TRS.SS.C2.P6)
  2028-02-23 → final exit: Aries 0° Ashwini Pada 1 PERMANENT (8:00 PM IST)
```

**[L1]** Saturn-natal-relationship map. Natal Saturn is in Libra 7H 22°27'. As transit Saturn moves, he casts 3rd/7th/10th aspects on:

| Transit sign | 3rd aspect → | 7th aspect → | 10th aspect → |
|---|---|---|---|

**The Aries transit's 10th aspect on Capricorn 10H** (2026-03-29 to 2026-07-26, then again 2027-04 onwards) lands DIRECTLY on:
- Sun (Shadbala #1) in 10H

- AL (Arudha Lagna)

This is a TRIPLE HIT from transit Saturn on the densest house in the chart, happening during natal Saturn AD. Classical tradition calls this "Saturn's double dristi" — transit Saturn aspecting the natal-and-dasha-activated domain — a CRITICAL period for the aspected house's themes.

**[L2 Kakshya-zone regime]** Of the 8 Pisces zones, 6 are INACTIVE (Z2/Z4/Z5/Z6/Z7/Z8) and 2 ACTIVE (Z1 Saturn's own, Z3 Mars's). Saturn traverses Pisces 0-30° back and forth. Zone coverage during 2026-04-16 to 2028-02-23 of Saturn's Pisces transits:
- 2026-09/10 through 2026-12-11: Saturn in Pisces ~29° → 22°-24° retrograde → Z7 (Moon ruler, INACTIVE) and Z8 (Lagna ruler, INACTIVE)

- 2027-10-20 → 2028-02-23: Saturn retrograde Pisces 28°-0° → Z8 INACTIVE moving through Z7 INACTIVE toward Z4 INACTIVE or Z3 ACTIVE if retrograde reaches ~9°

Practically, Saturn's Pisces occupancy in the 36-month window is almost entirely in INACTIVE zones. This is the memory-framework-validated "continuous wearing permission" for Saturn-strengthening remedies — consistent with v6.0 §8 zone classification.

**[L4 temporal stacking]** Saturn-transit crosses natal Saturn (Libra 22°27') via 7th aspect from Aries ~22°27' → happens 2027-07/08 approximately during Aries traversal ~22°-28° before retrograde. This is a **Saturn self-aspect return** and coincides with:
- Ketu MD imminent or just begun (Aug 21)
- Total Solar Eclipse Aug 2, 2027
- Chara Dasha already in Sco-Vir

A quadruple-significant convergence in Aug 2027.

**[L1]** Jupiter's 5/7/9 aspects from each sign onto natal houses:

| Leo 5H | Sagittarius 9H (natal Jupiter + Venus) | Aquarius 11H (natal Moon) | Aries 1H (Lagna) |

**Jupiter exaltation in Cancer (June-October 2026)** is the single most powerful transit in the 36-month window from an aspect-perspective:
- 7th aspect on 10H hits Sun + Mercury + AL (triple-hit) — amplifies CAREER / PUBLIC STATUS
- 9th aspect on 12H Pisces lands on the Chalit-Moon delivery (AK delivery point) — amplifies FOREIGN-INCOME architecture
- 5th aspect on 8H Scorpio hits natal Ketu — amplifies OCCULT / HIDDEN-ASSET dimensions

A single transit simultaneously activating the chart's three architectural layers (10H visible career, 12H delivery, 8H transformation) is exceptionally rare. Jupiter's 2nd exaltation pass (2027-04 to ~2027-07) provides a REPEAT of this triple-hit — which classical tradition reads as "what was initiated in the first pass ripens in the second."

**Leo transit 2026-10-31 → 2027-04 (with retrograde loop)** shifts aspects to:
- 7th on 11H → amplifies Moon, but Moon is already at 27° Aqu requiring Leo-27° for tight conjunction by opposition — happens only when Jupiter Leo reaches ~27°, which may not occur until Leo 2027 (2nd pass)
- 9th on 1H Lagna → amplifies LAGNA activation (Raja-Yoga-supporter from 9L Jupiter = his own natal house)
- 5th on 9H → amplifies 9H (his own natal placement) — Jupiter "self-amplification" period

**Virgo ingress 2028-06 (Jupiter DEBILITATION)** — a significant downshift. This is at the start of year 2 of Ketu MD. Jupiter debilitated in Virgo may receive Neecha Bhanga (Mercury in 10H Cap Vargottama + Mercury as dispositor of Virgo — Mercury is in Kendra from Lagna as 10H is kendra, so NBRY Jupiter-in-Virgo-cancelled-by-Mercury-in-kendra is a TRANSIT-NBRY).

### RPT.TRN.03 — Rahu-Ketu Transit Axis + Eclipse Hits

**[L0 → L5]**

**Rahu-Ketu axis path** (Lahiri sidereal):
- May 18, 2025 → Dec 5, 2026 (8:03 PM): Aquarius (Rahu) / Leo (Ketu)
- Dec 5, 2026 → ~June 2028: **Capricorn (Rahu) / Cancer (Ketu)**
- ~June 2028 → ~Nov 2029: Sagittarius (Rahu) / Gemini (Ketu)

**[L2]** Natal sensitive-point hits:
- Natal Sun 21°57' Capricorn: TRANSIT RAHU TRINES (trine = 120°) natal Sun via 9th aspect (Rahu's 9th aspect lands on Cap from Tau). When Rahu is in Capricorn (Dec 5 2026 → Jun 2028), transit Rahu physically COVERS natal Sun's sign — amplification, transformation, or disruption of 10L Sun.
- Natal Moon 27°02' Aquarius (PB3): transit Rahu in Aquarius (till Dec 5 2026) cast nodal proximity toward natal Moon at 27°; peak proximity was around mid-to-late 2025 to early 2026 when Rahu was in later degrees of Aquarius. Rahu in Aquarius throughout 2026 has been transiting CLOSE to natal Moon — this is the "Rahu's reach toward AK" phase. The nodal shift Dec 5 relieves this.
- Natal Rahu 19°01' Taurus / Ketu 19°01' Scorpio: Rahu return cycle is 18 years; natal is 1984, so next return 2002, 2020, 2038. NOT in 36-month window. However aspects: transit Ketu in Cancer (Dec 5 2026 → Jun 2028) casts 9th aspect on Pisces (12H), and casts 7th aspect on Capricorn 10H (natal Sun + Mercury territory) — a second Ketu hit on the 10H alongside Rahu.
- Bhrigu Bindu 8°04' Libra: transit Rahu casts 9th aspect (from Capricorn) on Libra via signs-away-120°? Cap + 120° = Tau (9th = Leo for standard signs). Actually Rahu's 9th aspect from Capricorn = Virgo (5 signs fwd) no—let me recount: Rahu's aspects classically are 5th, 7th, 9th forward. From Cap: 5th=Tau(2H),  7th=Cancer (4H), 9th=Virgo (6H). So Rahu-in-Cap does NOT aspect Libra/Bhrigu-Bindu directly. Ketu from Cancer: 5th=Scorpio(8H), 7th=Capricorn(10H), 9th=Pisces(12H). Ketu does not aspect Libra either.

This is a rare double-activation. Classical tradition (BPHS Ch.11, and the eclipse doctrine in Prashna Marga) treats eclipses on natal planets as "karmic openings" — the planet's natal promises become unusually accessible for the 6 months before and after the eclipse.
