### RPT.TRN.04 — Ashtakavarga Transit Model

**[L0 → L3]**

Transit benefit per Parashari BAV rule: a planet transiting a sign where its own BAV ≥5 is "beneficial window"; ≤2 is "challenge window"; 3-4 is "neutral".

```yaml
saturn_BAV_across_transit_signs_in_window:
  Pisces: 2 (CHALLENGE — Saturn's transit through own-BAV-2 = thin support)
  Aries: 4 (NEUTRAL)
  Taurus: 2 (CHALLENGE — for late-2028+ into Taurus transit after window)
  
jupiter_BAV_across_transit_signs:
  Gemini: 3 (NEUTRAL)
  Cancer: 4 (NEUTRAL — but Jupiter is exalted here, dignity compensates)
  Leo: 5 (BENEFICIAL — starting Oct 31 2026 and during retro return)
  Virgo: 6 (BENEFICIAL — despite Jupiter debilitation sign!)
  
rahu_BAV_(not_standard_in_Ashtakavarga):
  — nodes classically not BAV-scored; skip
```

**[L2]** Saturn's BAV-Pisces=2 is a structural "challenge window" reading across the entire Pisces traversal (about 30 of the 36 months). Pisces BAV contributors:
- Sun=2, Moon=6, Mars=2, Mer=3, Jup=4, Ven=4, Sat=2

Saturn gives only 2 bindus to Pisces. This reinforces CTR.01: Saturn's structural strength (Shadbala, Uccha) does not translate into transit-bindu support. The Sade-Sati setting phase carries low Saturn-support by Ashtakavarga — the Saturn transit is demanding, not consolidating.

**Jupiter's BAV-Cancer=4** is neutral on BAV metric BUT Jupiter is EXALTED in Cancer. Dignity compensates for mid-range bindu support. The net transit-amplification of Cancer Jupiter is driven by dignity, not by BAV.

**Jupiter's BAV-Virgo=6** is the HIGHEST Jupiter-BAV score of all 12 signs in this chart. When Jupiter enters Virgo (debilitation, 2028-06), the debilitation is PARTIALLY compensated by the high bindu support — an unusual pattern where the transit-sign SUPPORTS the debilitated planet.

**[L3]** The converging Ashtakavarga picture for the 36-month window:
- Saturn transits: mostly CHALLENGE-tier on his own BAV (Pisces 2, Aries 4) — demanding work-for-results posture
- Jupiter transits: peaks in BENEFICIAL-tier in Leo (5) and Virgo (6) — but Virgo is in 2028 post-Cancer window

For Jupiter-amplification-alignment with the harvest window (2026-06 to 2026-10 Cancer exaltation), BAV is only "neutral 4" — meaning the Jupiter-exaltation amplification operates THROUGH DIGNITY rather than through BAV-support. Effective but not maximum.

**[L4 temporal stacking]** Integrating BAV with the §D.5 heatmap critical-tier months:

- **2027-01 (Chara harvest gate)**: Saturn at Pisces ~22-23° (BAV 2 challenge) + Jupiter Cancer retrograde (BAV 4 neutral, dignity exalt). The harvest-gate month runs with CHALLENGE-tier Saturn-BAV and NEUTRAL Jupiter-BAV. Manifestation of harvest-opportunities will require Saturnine effort — "the gate opens but the weight is heavy."
- **2027-08 (Ketu MD + TSE)**: Saturn at Aries ~28° retrograde (BAV 4 neutral) + Jupiter Leo (BAV 5 beneficial). The regime-change month runs with NEUTRAL Saturn-BAV (improving from Pisces challenge) and BENEFICIAL Jupiter-BAV. Jupiter supports the Ketu-MD onset.
- **2028-02 (Saturn permanent Aries)**: Saturn at Aries 0° (BAV 4 neutral). Post-Sade-Sati phase opens with baseline-neutral Saturn-BAV — no amplification boost, no challenge deepening.

**[L5 contradiction check]** A real bindu-vs-dignity contradiction embedded in TRN.04: Jupiter's HIGHEST BAV sign (Virgo, 6) is his DEBILITATION sign. Jupiter's EXALTATION sign (Cancer) has only NEUTRAL BAV (4). This is a classical "dignity-vs-bindu inversion" — the native's chart supports Jupiter best when Jupiter is externally weak (debilitation + NBRY-rescue + BAV-strong) and less when Jupiter is externally strong (exaltation + mid-BAV). Interpretive implication: Jupiter-transit events during Virgo 2028-06+ may DELIVER MORE than Cancer-transit events 2026-06-10, despite the dignity-superiority of Cancer. The harvest-window aesthetic (dignity + transit aspect) is attractive but the DELIVERY aesthetic (bindu + NBRY) is different and may reward a different opportunity set.

#### DERIVATION_LEDGER (TRN.04)

```yaml
v6_ids_consumed: [AVG.BAV.SATURN (12 sign columns), AVG.BAV.JUPITER (12 sign columns), AVG.SAV.* (12 signs), AVG.SHP.*]
classical_rules_invoked:
  - rule: "Transit BAV threshold (BPHS Ch.67 Ashtakavarga)"
    application: "≥5 beneficial; ≤2 challenge; 3-4 neutral"
  - rule: "Dignity-vs-bindu inversion (classical interpretive doctrine)"
    application: "Jupiter Virgo debilitation with BAV 6 as second-order transit opportunity"
layers_traversed: [L0, L1, L2, L3, L4, L5]
```

#### WEAKNESS_AND_COUNTER_EVIDENCE (TRN.04)

```yaml
counter_evidence_from_v6:
  - id: AVG.BAV precision
    pushes_against: "Treating BAV thresholds as deterministic outcome predictors"
    magnitude: moderate
    note: "BAV thresholds (≥5 beneficial, ≤2 challenge) are classical heuristics, not mathematical truths. A planet with BAV 4 (neutral) can outperform a BAV 5 (beneficial) in the same chart if dignity, Kakshya, and dasha alignment differ. BAV is one input among many; the report's use of BAV to color critical-tier months is directional, not absolute."
  - id: AVG.BAV.SATURN.ARIES (4, neutral) during Saturn-AD + Ketu-MD overlap
    pushes_against: "Saturn's Aries transit as improving over Pisces"
    magnitude: minor
    note: "Saturn-BAV-Aries=4 is an improvement over Pisces=2 but still not beneficial-tier (≥5). The improvement is real but modest. Report's framing of 'Aries = baseline-neutral post-Sade-Sati' is appropriately calibrated."
  - id: AVG.BAV.JUPITER.VIRGO (6) + Jupiter debilitation (Virgo)
    pushes_against: "Simple dignity-or-bindu rule for Jupiter transit quality"
    magnitude: moderate
    note: "The Virgo-BAV-6-but-debilitation inversion is a genuine classical puzzle. The report resolves it toward 'second-order opportunity' reading, but alternative classical readings treat BAV as supporting-strength-of-significations rather than quality-of-outcome — under which reading, debilitation dominates. Confidence on the Virgo-2028 framing is moderate."
falsifiers:
  - if_observed: "Saturn's Pisces-transit periods produce qualitatively different outcomes (better or worse) than the 'BAV 2 challenge' framing predicts"
    check_by: ongoing review per transit milestone
    implication: "BAV may require re-weighting in the chart's overall transit model; Kakshya dominance may override BAV for this native."
confidence_after_critique: 0.70
```

### RPT.DEV.01 — Devata Architecture (Ishta / Dharma / Palana + Operational Variance)

**[L0 → L6]**

#### DEV.01.A — Classical derivation per v6.0 §20.1

```yaml
derivation_basis: Jaimini-classical
D9_Atmakaraka: Moon in Gemini (D9.MOON)
12th_from_AK_in_D9: Taurus → ruler Venus → Ishta Devata Mahalakshmi
9th_from_AK_in_D9: Aquarius → ruler Saturn → Dharma Devata Lord Venkateswara (Balaji)
AK_sign_in_D9: Gemini → ruler Mercury → Palana Devata Sri Krishna / Vishnu
```

#### DEV.01.B — Operational variance (per user memory framework)

Per memory-framework, Dharma Devata has been OPERATIONALLY refined to Lord Jagannath (Puri tradition) via a forensic argument rather than the classical Venkateswara. This is a legitimate interpretive divergence because:
- Classical rule identifies the PLANETARY-RULER of the Dharma-Devata seat (Saturn). Multiple iconographic traditions are mapped to Saturn as a planetary ruler. Venkateswara (Balaji) is one, but Jagannath (as a cosmic-disembodied form associated with Shani Shingnapur lineage, AND associated with the Aja-Ekapada / Purva Bhadrapada line through the Puri-Odisha tradition) is another.
- Geographic and personal resonance (Bhubaneswar birthplace, Odisha tradition) adds operational weight to Jagannath over Venkateswara.
- Per B.1 rule: v6.0 value (Venkateswara per classical derivation) is surfaced; operational-variant (Jagannath) is documented alongside.

Both paths are retained in this analysis. The worship effectiveness depends on which path the native's operative bhakti resonates with — a subjective-operational fact not derivable from chart data alone.

#### DEV.01.C — Secondary deity mappings (per v6.0 §20.2, §20.3)

```yaml
D10_Digpala: 
  - Lagna → Varuna (waters, 10H=West-Libra direction etc)
  - Sun (10L) → Yama (discipline)
  - Saturn (10H occupant) → Isana (Shiva-form, NE)
D20_Sadhana:
  - Lagna → Jvalamukhi (devi of fire — D20 sadhana sign-lord pairing)
  - Moon → Tripurasundari (Moon's sadhana presiding devata per tradition)
D24_Education:
  - Lagna → Govinda
  - Mercury (karaka) → Bhima (strength)
  - Jupiter → Antaka (yama-form)
```

The D20 Moon-Tripurasundari assignment is significant — Sri Vidya / Tripurasundari worship is an auxiliary devata path specifically for Moon-AK-in-12H architecture. Tripurasundari is a Lalita-form, closely associated with the Mahalakshmi-Ishta through Kamakoti/Sri-chakra tradition.

#### DEV.01.D — Activation windows for each devata

| Devata | Planetary ruler | Activation via Dasha | Activation via Transit |
|---|---|---|---|
| Mahalakshmi (Ishta) | Venus | Venus MD 2034-08-21; Venus AD in Ketu MD 2028-01-18 → 2029-03-18 | Venus transits of 10H/12H/Lagna |
| Jagannath/Venkateswara (Dharma) | Saturn | Saturn AD current (2024-12 → 2027-08); Yogini Ulka 2026-12 → 2032-12 | Saturn transit aspects on natal Sun (2026-04 to 2027-08 via 10th aspect from Aries) |
| Sri Krishna (Palana) | Mercury | Mercury MD current (through 2027-08); Mercury AD multiple future | Mercury transits through 10H Cap (annually) |
| Tripurasundari (D20 Moon) | Moon | Moon AD in future MDs; Yogini Mangala 2047 | Moon transits of Aquarius / Chalit-12 timing |

#### DEV.01.E — [L6 Intervention synthesis]

The devata-intervention hierarchy for the 2026-2029 window:
1. **PRIMARY: Mahalakshmi** (Ishta) — direct and sustained; the chart-specified primary pathway
2. **SECONDARY-DHARMA: Jagannath/Venkateswara** (operational vs classical) — ACTIVE now through Saturn AD and Yogini Ulka; peak potency 2026-12 through 2032-12
3. **SUPPORTING: Sri Krishna / Vishnu** (Palana) — Mercury MD residual through 2027-08; post-MD, Krishna worship continues via chart-architecture but loses dasha-activation until Mercury-antardashas in later MDs
4. **AUXILIARY: Tripurasundari** (D20 Moon) — always-appropriate for Moon-AK-12H charts; intensify during Moon-related sub-periods

The memory-framework timing of the Jul 16, 2026 Rath Yatra Jagannath Sudarshana-Lakshmi Maha Homam aligns with:
- Jupiter exalted in Cancer (transit)
- Mercury-Saturn AD (Vimshottari)
- Bhadrika Yogini (Mercury) still active (5 months before Ulka transition)
- Chara Sco-Lib still running
- Pre-combust Jupiter (Jul 14 combust start — so Jul 16 is 2 days INTO combust; worship should address this caveat — traditional Rath Yatra timing is fixed to Ashadha Shukla Dwitiya regardless of Jupiter-combust status)
- Jagannath himself is not a Jupiter-deity — he is Saturn/Vishnu composite per operational framework, so Jupiter-combust is less directly disruptive to Jagannath-specific worship

#### DEV.01.F — Three-Interpretation Enumeration (Devata architecture)

Per §A.1: the devata assignment admits competing readings, especially the Dharma Devata (Venkateswara classical vs Jagannath operational).

```yaml
interpretation_A_memory_framework_triad:
  claim: "Mahalakshmi primary (Ishta) + Jagannath operational-secondary (Dharma) + Krishna supporting (Palana) + Tripurasundari auxiliary (D20 Moon). This is the memory-framework's integrated devata architecture; Jagannath replaces classical Venkateswara on operational grounds (geographic affinity, native's Odisha tradition, Saturn-Vishnu composite reading)."
  supporting_evidence:
    - Classical 12th-from-AK-in-D9 rule yields Taurus → Venus → Mahalakshmi (confirmed)
    - Classical AK-sign-in-D9 rule yields Gemini → Mercury → Krishna/Vishnu (confirmed)
    - Classical 9th-from-AK-in-D9 rule yields Aquarius → Saturn (ruler)
    - Saturn-ruled deity tradition admits multiple forms; regional Odisha tradition maps Jagannath to Saturn-ruler-role
    - MET.BIRTH.PLACE Bhubaneswar + native's Odisha heritage gives operational-resonance weight to Jagannath
    - Jagannath worship at Puri is currently Saturn-AD activated (AD lord = Saturn; Jagannath = Saturn-operational-form)
    - Operational-overlays on classical derivations are legitimate within Jaimini tradition (Sanjay Rath teaching corpus explicitly accommodates regional-devata refinement)

interpretation_B_strict_classical_venkateswara:
  claim: "Classical derivation yields Venkateswara (Balaji) as Dharma Devata. The operational-override to Jagannath is interpretive overlay NOT derivable from v6.0 alone. Strict Jaimini-classical reading returns Venkateswara. The report should not privilege operational-override over classical-derivation when the goal is chart-fidelity."
  supporting_evidence:
    - v6.0 §20.1 classical derivation explicitly yields Venkateswara
    - Saturn-ruler = Balaji / Venkateswara is the MAINSTREAM classical assignment (B.V. Raman, K.N. Rao, most published sources)
    - Jagannath as Saturn-composite is a SECONDARY tradition, not primary
    - Methodology rigor: operational-overrides introduce subjective-interpretive noise into what should be chart-derived architecture
    - Venkateswara worship during Saturn AD still fulfills Dharma-devata-activation requirement
    - Native can engage Jagannath AS WELL as Venkateswara, but the PRIMARY Dharma-path per v6.0 derivation is Venkateswara

interpretation_C_equal_tri_deity_activation:
  claim: "All three deities (Ishta/Dharma/Palana) receive EQUAL-priority daily worship. Dasha-temporal hierarchy (currently prioritizing Dharma via Saturn AD) is a minor modulation, not a primary re-ranking. The classical Jaimini doctrine treats Ishta/Dharma/Palana as a permanent triad, not as a ranked hierarchy that shifts with dasha."
  supporting_evidence:
    - Jaimini classical text does not specify dasha-based re-ranking of Ishta/Dharma/Palana; it describes them as permanent structural roles
    - Ishta is ALWAYS primary (by definition) regardless of dasha — but the secondary ranking of Dharma vs Palana in classical text is not explicit
    - Modern practitioner-corpora (Sanjay Rath, Ernst Wilhelm) often SUGGEST dasha-activation-shifting but do not MANDATE it
    - Equal-triad worship may prevent any single-devata-dependency becoming a spiritual-single-point-of-failure
    - Native's wellbeing benefits from broad-spectrum spiritual practice rather than dasha-narrow focus

evidence_weighing:
  - A vs B: Methodological debate. A accepts operational-overlay; B enforces chart-strict derivation. Neither is empirically falsifiable at short time-horizons (deity-worship outcomes are subjective-spiritual, not objective-measurable). A's geographic-resonance argument is real but extra-chart; B's chart-fidelity argument is real but ignores regional-tradition weight.
  - A + C vs B: A and C differ on DASHA-TEMPORAL RANKING within the triad. A says 'current Saturn AD privileges Dharma'; C says 'triad is permanent, no re-ranking.' This is a soft disagreement; both accept the underlying triad.
  - B vs classical literature: Strict classical literature does yield Venkateswara. Readers prioritizing methodological rigor should default to B. Readers prioritizing operational-resonance may prefer A.
  - The native's memory-framework has already elected A. Operationally, the worship is already happening under A's framing. The report has no basis to override the native's operational choice.

chosen_interpretation: "A (memory-framework triad) as operational-primary, with B (strict-classical-Venkateswara) preserved as methodologically-authoritative alternative + C (equal-triad) as breadth-of-practice fallback."
rationale: >
  The native's operational choice (Jagannath-operational as Dharma-Devata) is legitimate within
  Jaimini-tradition regional-overlay practice and is already in active worship per memory-framework.
  The report retains the classical derivation (Venkateswara) as ALSO-VALID and notes that any
  future disruption of Jagannath-path worship (e.g., relocation away from Odisha, operational
  pragmatic shifts) can revert to classical Venkateswara without loss of chart-fidelity.
  C's equal-triad reading is the safest breadth-posture if the native wishes to avoid
  dasha-narrow-specialization and prefers sustained tri-deity practice.
  The Ishta (Mahalakshmi) is non-negotiable PRIMARY across all three interpretations.
  Operational implication: continue current Mahalakshmi-primary + Jagannath-secondary + Krishna-
  supporting practice. Rath Yatra 2026-07-16 Maha Homam is appropriate under A; if B-oriented,
  a Venkateswara-homam at a Venkateswara-temple (Tirumala or any local Balaji shrine) during
  the same Sat-AD window would serve the equivalent function.

interpretation_risk_B_methodological_preference: >
  If the reader is methodologically strict (privileges v6.0 chart-fidelity over operational-overlay),
  they should substitute Venkateswara for Jagannath in all Dharma-references. This is a legitimate
  reader-posture; the report documents both paths.

falsifier_for_chosen:
  - if_observed: "Sustained Mahalakshmi + Jagannath + Krishna worship across 2026-2028 produces no discernible spiritual alignment or material-goal support"
    check_by: 2028-08-21
    implication: "Either the triad framework is mis-derived OR the Venus-weakness (SBL.TOTAL.VENUS 4.60) dominates Ishta-effectiveness more than anticipated. Reconsider: switch to strict-Venkateswara (B), intensify Mahalakshmi-direct (bypass the weak Venus-intercessor via direct-Lakshmi-formulae), or accept that spiritual-material-alignment requires longer horizon than 30 months."
confidence_in_selection: 0.75
```

### RPT.KAK.01 — Saturn Kakshya Zones Full Forensic (v6.0 §8 consumed in entirety)

**[L0 → L6]**

#### KAK.01.A — Zone Map (direct from v6.0 §8)

```yaml
pisces_kakshya_zones:
```

**[L2 interpretation]** The zone map confirms the chart-specific finding that Saturn's Pisces transit is OPERATIONALLY DAMPED for this native across 75% of the sign. Only when Saturn transits the first 3°45' (Z1, own-zone-of-Saturn) or the 7°30'–11°15' arc (Z3, Mars-ruled) does the transit register as karmically-active.

The ACTIVE zones (Z1 + Z3) are precisely the Saturn-own-domain and the Mars-ruled arc. Classical interpretation: Saturn transit-activation peaks when Saturn is either (a) in his own natural arc (self-referential intensification) or (b) in Mars-flavored arcs (Saturn-Mars karmic-friction-activation, consistent with natal Mars+Saturn conjunction in 7H Libra within 7.38° orb).

**[L3 temporal trace]** Saturn's Pisces degree-path through 36-month window mapped to zone occupancy:

```yaml

    zone_applicability: NA (Aries permanent; Pisces Kakshya map no longer active)

```

**[L4 temporal stacking with other systems]** Zone-active windows overlaid with other dasha-transit activations:

| Estimated window | Zone ACTIVE | Co-occurring activations | Composite severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| Late 2027 – early 2028 | Z3 Mars | Sade Sati P6 final phase + Aries transition pending | Moderate — Mars-Saturn activation during Sade-Sati closure |
| Feb 2028 final weeks | Z1 Saturn | Sade Sati P6 ending + Saturn preparing permanent Aries | Moderate-high — Saturn self-zone during Sade-Sati closure |

**[L5 contradiction / paradox resolution]** A potential paradox: if 75% of the Pisces transit is INACTIVE and the memory-framework interprets this as "benign Saturn-transit with continuous Iron Ring wearing permission," why does Sade Sati classical doctrine treat the entire Pisces phase as karmically-loaded?

Resolution: Kakshya zone INACTIVE ≠ Sade Sati phase-benign. The two are orthogonal frameworks operating at different granularities. Sade Sati is a coarse-grained 7.5-year karmic phase operating at the sign-from-Moon level; Kakshya zones are fine-grained transit-severity modulations at the 3°45' zone level. INACTIVE Kakshya REDUCES transit-damage within a Sade-Sati phase but does NOT negate the phase-level karmic pressure. Both effects compound additively rather than canceling.

**[L6 intervention leverage]** Derived operational protocol:

- **Iron Ring continuous wearing**: authorized for the 75% INACTIVE coverage. Specific remove-or-review windows: late 2027 Z3 Mars activation (~2-3 weeks) + Feb 2028 Z1 Saturn activation (~2-3 weeks before permanent Aries exit).
- **Blue Sapphire**: remains CONTRAINDICATED regardless of zone status (per INT.02 + CTR.01 Shuddha-Pinda-weakness).
- **Mars-propitiation synergy**: during Z3 activation windows, intensify Mangala-propitiation (Hanuman Chalisa, Subrahmanya worship) to channel Mars-Saturn friction constructively.
- **Saturn-propitiation intensity**: during Z1 activation windows, intensify Shani-propitiation (Shani-stotra, Jagannath worship as Dharma-devata-operational-form) to channel Saturn self-intensification.

```yaml
v6_ids_consumed: [KAK.PISCES.Z1, KAK.PISCES.Z2, KAK.PISCES.Z3, KAK.PISCES.Z4, KAK.PISCES.Z5, KAK.PISCES.Z6, KAK.PISCES.Z7, KAK.PISCES.Z8, PLN.SATURN (natal Libra), PLN.MARS (natal Libra conjunct Saturn), TRS.SS.C2.P5, TRS.SS.C2.P6, external Saturn ephemeris]
```

### RPT.SAH.01 — Tajika Sahams (All Six) Forensic

**[L0 → L5]**

v6.0 §12.2 populates all six classical Tajika Sahams for day-birth (native born 1984-02-05 10:43 IST, Sun above horizon = day birth). Each Saham's placement is traced to chart architecture and cross-referenced with existing signatures.

#### SAH.01.A — Saham Inventory + Architectural Convergences

```yaml
- id: SAH.PUNYA
  saham: Punya
  theme: "Fortune / Spiritual Merit"
  result_abs_long: 47.48°
  sign: Taurus
  degree: 17°28′
  house_from_lagna: 2

  nakshatra_pada: 3 (approximate, derivable from 17°28')
```

#### SAH.01.B — Saham Grid (quick-reference cross-sign-house table)

| Saham | Sign | House | Major Co-location | Dominant Archetype |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Punya | Taurus | 2 | Rahu | Fortune via unconventional Rahu-channels |
| Rajya | Aries | 1 | Lagna (3°57' sep) | Authority from self-constitution |
| Karma | Aquarius | 11 | Moon-sign (27° sep) | Action aligned with soul-purpose (AK-sign-share) |
| Labha | Sagittarius | 9 | Jupiter+Venus | Gain via Lakshmi Yoga seat (dharmic-wealth) |
| Vivaha | Gemini | 3 | UL+A5+A11 | Marriage at UL-seat with Ardra/Rahu-flavor |
| Putra | Capricorn | 10 | Sun (3°13' sep)+AL | Children bound to career-density |

#### SAH.01.C — Aggregate Architecture Reading

All six Sahams land at architecturally-significant loci — this is NOT statistical noise. Specifically:

1. **Punya co-locates with Rahu** → Fortune is Rahu-flavored (unconventional)
2. **Rajya sits near Lagna** → Authority is self-constituted
3. **Karma shares sign with AK-Moon** → Action carries soul-purpose weight
4. **Labha co-locates with Jupiter+Venus in 9H** → Gains arrive via Lakshmi-Yoga seat
5. **Vivaha lands at UL** → Marriage-signifier validates UL-partnership-axis
6. **Putra co-locates with Sun in 10H AL** → Children bound to career-visibility axis

The Saham-grid provides a SECOND INDEPENDENT CONFIRMATION of the chart's architectural conclusions already derived from other systems. The Mercury-Yogi / Moon-AK / 9H-Lakshmi / 10H-career architecture is triply-supported: by natal placement, by Karakamsa, and now by Saham distribution.

**[L5 contradiction check]** A possible contradiction: if Vivaha Saham places marriage-signifier at UL/A11/A5 trio in Gemini (3H, Mercury-ruled), why does HSE.02 treat 7H as the fragile partnership axis?

Resolution: Vivaha Saham signifies marriage-FORMATION locus (initial connection, karma-arranged meeting); 7H signifies marriage-SUSTAINED locus (lived relationship, partnership-contract). A marriage can be FORMED via strong Saham-Gemini-Rahu-flavored karmic encounter AND simultaneously be SUSTAINED under 7H-Sasha-Yoga-in-weak-Bhavabala structural friction. The two readings describe different life-stages of the same institution, not contradictory states.

#### WEAKNESS_AND_COUNTER_EVIDENCE (SAH.01)

```yaml
counter_evidence_from_v6:
  - id: Saham-convergence interpretation universality
    pushes_against: "Treating all 6 Sahams as architecturally meaningful"
    magnitude: moderate
    note: "Sahams are DERIVED points; their formulas involve multiple planets summed modulo 360°. It is NOT rare for at least some Sahams to land near natal bodies simply by the density of natal placements in certain signs (here Capricorn, Sagittarius, Aquarius all populated). The Saham-grid's impressiveness may partly reflect natal-density rather than specifically-meaningful Saham-alignment."
  - id: Day-birth vs Night-birth formula ambiguity at borderline TOB
    pushes_against: "Saham result precision"
    magnitude: minor
    note: "Native's TOB 10:43 IST with sunrise ~6:18 is firmly day-birth (4h25m after sunrise). No formula-selection ambiguity. However, if TOB rectification ever moves birth-time by hours, day/night determination could flip for a boundary case (not applicable here)."
falsifiers:
  - if_observed: "Life-events categorically fail to align with Saham-signaled domains (Labha Saham at Lakshmi-seat but gains consistently arrive via non-9H channels; Putra Saham at 10H but children entirely separate from career; etc.)"
    check_by: rolling observation across 5+ years
    implication: "Saham doctrine under-predicts for this native; chart should be read without Saham weighting."
confidence_after_critique: 0.75
```

### RPT.UPG.01 — Upagrahas Forensic (All Nine)

**[L0 → L5]**

v6.0 §11.1 populates all nine upagrahas (4 time-based + 5 Sun-based) with sign, degree, nakshatra. Each is now traced to natal architecture with tight-conjunction and aspect-geometry analysis.

#### UPG.01.B — Tight Upagraha-Natal Conjunctions (Priority Summary)

| Rank | Upagraha | Natal body | Separation | Significance |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Vyatipata (Sun-shadow) | Sun 10L (Cap 10H AL) | **2°45′** | TIGHT — calamity-passing shadow at career/authority seat |
| 2 | Upaketu (Ketu-shadow) | Venus (Sag 9H) | **2°47′** | TIGHT — moksha/detachment shadow at Ishta-ruler |
| 3 | Ardhaprahara (Venus's-son) | Lagna (Aries) | **1°31′** | TIGHT — Venus-aesthetic thread built into self-identity |
| 4 | Indrachapa (Sun-rainbow) | Jupiter (Sag 9H) | **4°31′** | CLOSE — benefic-shadow at Lakshmi-Yoga-9L seat |
| 5 | Mandi (Saturn's-son) | (opposition to Sun 10H) | 7°44′ (by aspect) | MODERATE — aspect-based shadow on career-axis |

Three of the five major upagraha-hits cluster on the **authority/Lagna/Venus axis**. This is a SIGNATURE: the chart's identity-expression (Lagna) + public-authority (Sun 10H) + Ishta-pathway (Venus) all carry specific upagraha-karmic-shadows that are neither pathological nor purely benefic but introduce subtle moksha/dispassion/calamity-passing threads into their operations.

#### UPG.01.C — Synthesis: The Upagraha Pattern

The upagraha distribution produces three architectural insights:

1. **Venus-axis is Upagraha-loaded**: Ardhaprahara on Lagna (Venus's-son), Upaketu on Venus (moksha-shadow), Indrachapa on Jupiter (benefic-shadow on Lakshmi seat). Venus-signification throughout the chart carries "detached-refinement" flavor — aligned with the Ishta-Devata (Mahalakshmi) path's spiritual requirement for non-gripping devotion.

2. **Career-axis is Vyatipata-shadowed**: Sun 10H AL carries "calamity-passing" upagraha within 2°45'. Classical reading: public-role is tested by recurring near-crises that DO NOT destroy the role — they refine it. This is consistent with Saturn-AD structural testing (SIG.01) and with "career forged through adversity" patterns.

3. **Partnership-axis is Gulika-shadowed**: Gulika at UL Gemini = shadow-Saturn at marriage-formation-locus. Consistent with HSE.02 7H fragility reading, provides additional layer on the karmic-complexity of partnership in this chart.

No upagraha lands tightly on the 11H-12H foreign-income architecture — that axis is upagraha-CLEAR. This is architecturally favorable: the chart's primary wealth-channel (12H-mediated, via Moon-AK-Chalit-12 + D9 stellium) is NOT shadowed by any upagraha, distinguishing it from the partnership/career axes which ARE upagraha-shadowed.

#### WEAKNESS_AND_COUNTER_EVIDENCE (UPG.01)

```yaml
counter_evidence_from_v6:
  - id: Upagraha doctrine variability across schools
    pushes_against: "Confidence in upagraha-based interpretations"
    magnitude: moderate
    note: "Classical Jyotish literature has LESS consensus on upagraha-based predictive weight than on planet/house/dasha doctrine. Some schools (Parashari mainstream) use them peripherally; others (some Tantric/Tajika/Jaimini blends) give them significant weight. The findings here are ADDITIVE overlays to the primary architectural conclusions, not primary drivers."
  - id: Sun-based upagraha position precision
    pushes_against: "Tight-conjunction claims for Sun-based upagrahas"
    magnitude: minor
    note: "Sun-based upagrahas are derived from Sun's longitude + fixed additives; precision is identical to natal Sun precision (which is ephemeris-accurate). Time-based upagrahas depend on birth-time precision. All positions in v6.0 §11.1 inherit v6.0 MET precision."
falsifiers:
  - if_observed: "Life-events at career-authority axis (Sun-10H) show no pattern of 'calamity-passing' (recurring near-crises that test-but-do-not-destroy)"
    check_by: 2029-04-16 (sufficient longitudinal sample)
    implication: "Vyatipata-Sun doctrine is over-weighted for this native; re-read upagraha analysis as peripheral overlay."
  - if_observed: "Relationship/partnership outcomes show CLEAN delivery with no shadow-thread patterns matching Gulika-UL signature"
    check_by: ongoing relational observation
    implication: "Upagraha-UL doctrine under-predicts; HSE.02 7H fragility framing captures partnership-architecture without upagraha-layer being needed."
confidence_after_critique: 0.72
```

### RPT.VAR.01 — Varshphal 2026-27 Year Lord Computation and Architectural Implications

**[L0 → L6]**

v6.0 §22 populated three of five Varshphal fields (Validity 2026-02-05 to 2027-02-05; Muntha Sign Libra; Muntha Lord Venus) and left two fields pending (Year Lord; Mudda Dasha) as "requires exact solar return time." This section computes the Year Lord via Tajika Pancha-Vargiya Bala across the five classical Varshesha candidates, using v6.0 natal data + external ephemeris date verification.

#### VAR.01.A — The Five Varshesha Candidates (Tajika Pancha-adhikari rule)

Tajika classical rule (Neelakantha Tajika, Tajika Nilakanthi): The Year Lord (Varshesha) is the strongest of FIVE candidates, where strength is scored via Pancha-Vargiya Bala (5 divisional strengths). The five candidates:

```yaml
varshesha_candidates:
  - candidate: Janma-Lagnesh
    identity: "Mars (lord of natal Aries Lagna)"
    v6_source: [MET.LAGNA (Aries), PLN.MARS]
    natal_profile:
      - D1: Libra 18°31' 7H (enemy sign, kendra-from-kendra)
      - Shadbala: 7.39 Rupas (rank 5)
      - Shuddha Pinda: 198 (rank 1 — CHART HIGHEST)
      - Vimsopaka: 11.8 (rank 2)
      - Avastha: Swapna / Vradha / Deepta
    pancha_vargiya_sketch: "Own-sign (Sva): Libra is enemy → 0; Uccha: far from Cancer 28° exalt → low; Drekkana/Navamsa/Hadda: mixed. Composite moderate."

  - candidate: Muntha Lord
    identity: "Venus (lord of Libra — the Muntha sign for 2026-27 per v6.0 VRS.MUNTHA.LORD)"
    v6_source: [VRS.MUNTHA.SIGN (Libra), VRS.MUNTHA.LORD (Venus), PLN.VENUS]
    natal_profile:
      - D1: Sagittarius 19°10' 9H (friendly sign)
      - Shadbala: 4.60 Rupas (rank 7 WEAKEST — below min 5.50)
      - Shuddha Pinda: not chart-top (rank 5, mid)
      - Vimsopaka: 9.5 (rank 6)
      - Avastha: Jagratadi / Kumara / Deena
    pancha_vargiya_sketch: "Own-sign: not own; Uccha: far from Pisces 27° exalt; overall WEAK. Low Tajika composite."

  - candidate: Trirashi Lord (triplicity lord for Varshphal Lagna's element, day-birth)
    identity: "Depends on Varshphal Lagna element — not knowable without exact solar return time"
    v6_source: (pending)
    possible_values:
      - If Varshphal Lagna is Fire (Ar/Le/Sag) day-birth: Sun
      - If Earth (Ta/Vi/Cap) day-birth: Venus
      - If Air (Ge/Li/Aq) day-birth: Saturn
      - If Water (Ca/Sc/Pi) day-birth: Venus
    computational_hint: "Solar return for native (sidereal Sun return to 21°57' Capricorn Lahiri) falls approximately 2026-02-05 at or near birth-hour-equivalent. Without exact ephemeris-second precision, Varshphal Lagna is estimated with ±1 sign uncertainty."

  - candidate: Varsha-Lagnesh
    identity: "Lord of the Varshphal-Lagna (sign rising at solar return moment at native's current location)"
    v6_source: (pending)
    computational_hint: "Native's current location assumed Bhubaneswar per MET.BIRTH.PLACE. Solar return Feb 5 2026 approximately mid-morning (matching TOB 10:43 IST) likely yields Aries, Taurus, or Gemini rising. Most likely Aries (same as natal Lagna) with ruler = Mars; less likely Taurus (ruler Venus) or Gemini (ruler Mercury). Uncertainty ±1 sign."

  - candidate: Dina-Swami (Day Lord / Varesh — weekday of solar return)
    identity: "Jupiter (Thursday 2026-02-05 confirmed Thursday = Guruvara)"
    v6_source: (external confirmation: 2026-02-05 = Thursday)
    natal_profile:
      - D1: Sagittarius 09°48' 9H (OWN SIGN — Sva)
      - Shadbala: 7.73 Rupas (rank 4 — above min 6.50)
      - Shuddha Pinda: mid-rank
      - Vimsopaka: 12.1 (rank 1 — CHART HIGHEST)
      - Avastha: (check)
      - Uccha Bala: 8.40 (rank 7 LAST — weak Uccha)
    pancha_vargiya_sketch: "Own-sign (Sva): YES = +max; Vargottama: NOT Vargottama in D9 (Jup in D9 Gemini); Hadda: moderate; Drekkana: moderate; Navamsa: Gemini (not-Jup-ruled). Composite: HIGH due to Sva + Vimsopaka rank-1 dominance."
```

#### VAR.01.B — Pancha-Vargiya Bala Ranking

Tajika Pancha-Vargiya Bala scores each candidate across 5 divisional strengths. Approximate composite (scaled 0-100) for the three known candidates + best-case estimates for the two pending:

| Candidate | Sva (own-sign) | Hadda | Drekkana | Navamsa | Dignity/Uccha | Composite | Rank |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Jupiter (Day Lord Thursday) | 20 (own Sagittarius) | 10 (mid) | 10 (mid) | 5 (Gemini D9 not-Jup) | 5 (Uccha weak) | **50** | 1 (likely) |
| Mars (Janma Lagnesh) | 0 (Libra enemy) | 10 (mid) | 10 (mid) | 15 (Scorpio D9 own-sign — Vargottama-adjacent) | 8 (mid) | **43** | 3 |
| Venus (Muntha Lord) | 0 (Sag not-own) | 8 (mid) | 8 (mid) | 10 (Virgo D9 debil) | 3 (Uccha weak) | **29** | 4 (likely) |
| Trirashi Lord (pending) | estimate 10 | — | — | — | — | ~30-40 | 3-4 |
| Varsha-Lagnesh (pending) | estimate 10 | — | — | — | — | ~30-40 | 3-4 |

**Jupiter (Day Lord, Thursday weekday) is the MOST LIKELY Year Lord** of the 2026-27 Varshphal. Confidence 0.72 given pending exact-time candidates.

#### VAR.01.C — Architectural Implications of Jupiter-as-Year-Lord

If Jupiter is the Varshesha for 2026-02-05 to 2027-02-05, the entire year is Jupiter-colored. Consequences:

```yaml
jupiter_year_lord_implications:
  yoga_alignment:
    - Lakshmi Yoga (SIG.08, CYSS 77): Jupiter is 9L member → Varshesha activates 9L-wealth-pathway for the year
    - Saraswati Yoga (SIG.07, CYSS 91): Jupiter is member → Varshesha supports knowledge-wealth channel
    - Hamsa MPY (absent per YOG.01.B, needed Jupiter in kendra — FAILS 9H-is-trikona-not-kendra): not amplified
  transit_alignment:
    - Jupiter Cancer exaltation Jun 2 2026 to Oct 31 2026 runs WITHIN the Varshphal validity window (Feb 5 2026 to Feb 5 2027). VARSHESH IS EXALTED IN TRANSIT for 5 months of his own year.
    - Jupiter's second Cancer exaltation pass ~2027-04 falls OUTSIDE this Varshphal year (next year)
    - Jupiter's 7th aspect from exalted Cancer lands on 10H Cap Sun+Mercury+AL during his year-lordship — DIRECT YEAR-LORD AMPLIFICATION of career-density axis
  dasha_alignment:
    - Current Mer MD + Sat AD (through 2027-08) — neither is Jupiter, so Year-Lord-Jupiter operates as an OVERLAY on the prevailing Vimshottari, not a dominant driver
    - Jupiter PD within Mer-Sat AD estimated 2027-04-22 to 2027-08-21 per DSH.01.B — this sub-period falls at the END of the 2026-27 Varshphal year and extends into next year
  muntha_coherence:
    - Muntha in Libra 7H, Muntha Lord Venus (weak)
    - Year Lord Jupiter CASTS 5TH ASPECT on Aries 1H from Sag 9H natally — supporting self/Lagna dimension while Muntha tests the partnership axis
    - Year Lord Jupiter does NOT aspect 7H Libra (Jupiter's 5/7/9 aspects from Sag miss Libra) — Jupiter-Year-Lord provides SUPPORT TO SELF but NOT TO MUNTHA-SIGN directly. Operational implication: the native must personally bridge Year-Lord-Jupiter's support to Muntha-Libra's focus — i.e., consciously apply Jupiter-wisdom/dharma to Libra-partnership/balance themes.

varshphal_year_theme:
  primary: "Dharma-wealth + knowledge-pathway year with exalted-transit amplification; authority-platform strengthening via Jupiter's 7th aspect to 10H"
  secondary: "Muntha-in-fragile-7H tests partnership; but Year-Lord Jupiter does not aspect 7H — partnership-tests must be navigated through self-effort (Jupiter's 5th aspect on Lagna)"
  tertiary: "Jupiter-combust Jul 14-Aug 12 2026 INTERRUPTS Year-Lord potency for 30 days mid-year; combust-period requires Brihaspati-Gayatri mitigation"
```

#### VAR.01.D — Mudda Dasha (Tajika Annual Dasha) — Structural Framework

The Mudda Dasha system distributes 365 days across the 9 Vimshottari planets in proportional sub-periods. Without exact solar return time, the opening-Mudda can be estimated:

```yaml
mudda_dasha_framework:
  rule: "Year opens with Year-Lord's Mudda (most common Tajika tradition) OR with the Patyayini Mudda sequence starting from Lagnesh"
  if_jupiter_is_year_lord:
    opening_mudda: Jupiter Mudda (~48 days assuming proportional to Vimshottari 16/120 × 365 = 48.67 days)
    jupiter_mudda_window: 2026-02-05 to approximately 2026-03-25
    second_mudda: Saturn Mudda (~58 days, 2026-03-25 to 2026-05-22)
    full_sequence_pending: exact solar return time required for precise boundaries
  architectural_note: "The opening-Jupiter-Mudda overlaps with natal Saturn transiting Aries (per TRN.01) and Sun transiting its own 10H Capricorn sign-ruler period. The year literally opens with Year-Lord exercising his initial sub-period."
```

Full computation of all 9 Muddas requires exact solar return timestamp; this report provides the structural framework rather than full boundary resolution.

#### VAR.01.E — [L6 Intervention Leverage]

Varshphal-specific interventions for the 2026-02-05 to 2027-02-05 window:

1. **Jupiter propitiation** during Jupiter-Mudda (approx Feb-Mar 2026) and through the year as Varshesh — intensify Guru-worship, Jupiter mantra, Brihaspati-Gayatri, Jupiter-yantra
2. **Mitigate Jupiter combust** Jul 14 – Aug 12 2026 — during this 30-day mid-year window, Year-Lord is energetically-reduced. Worship intensifies rather than reduces during combust (classical rule: weak lords receive more propitiation, not less).
3. **Muntha-Libra-Venus year-long attention** — since Muntha is in fragile Libra-7H and ruled by weakest Venus, this is a year where relationship/partnership axis requires explicit care. Do NOT expect Year-Lord-Jupiter to auto-compensate for 7H weakness.
4. **Rath Yatra Maha Homam (Jul 16 2026)** — per DEV.01 and INT.03, falls in this Varshphal year and aligns with Jupiter-Cancer-exaltation and Year-Lord-activation (even during combust). Memory-framework timing is Varshphal-year-coherent.
5. **Varshphal-year-end transition (Feb 2027)** — the subsequent Varshphal 2027-28 will have a DIFFERENT Year Lord (solar return falls on a different weekday Feb 5 2027 = Friday per calendar, so Day Lord would become Venus; but full computation requires 2027-specific verification). This means transition-of-year may shift Varshesha from Jupiter to Venus — intensifying Ishta-Devata-ruler activation at the year-transition.

```yaml
  closed: TRUE

    authority-delivery depends on Jupiter's dharmic-grounding, which depends on Ketu's
    transformative-dissolution, which depends on Saturn's structural-discipline. None operates
    independently. The triangle means the upcoming Ketu-MD (Aug 2027) does NOT sever Saturn's
    influence — it carries Saturn-quality forward through the nakshatra-link, while simultaneously
    activating Jupiter's nakshatra-lord (Ketu) as the dominant temporal lord. The regime change
    at Aug 2027 is therefore less abrupt at the nakshatra level than it appears at the Vimshottari
    dasha level.
```

### RPT.AUD.05 — Ashtakavarga BAV Forensic Analysis

**[Audit Pass 2, 2026-04-16]**

```yaml
bav_key_patterns:

  mercury_bav_highlights:
    - "Mercury BAV on Taurus (2H) = 7 (Mercury's JOINT-HIGHEST). The MD lord gives maximum bindu-support to the wealth-house. Despite 2H Bhavabala being weak (rank 11), Mercury provides strong BAV support — meaning Mercury-MD-related wealth CAN accumulate in 2H if effort is applied."
    - "Mercury BAV on Scorpio (8H) = 7 (tied highest). The MD lord also maximally supports the 8H-transformation house (where Ketu sits). Mercury MD's best legacy is 8H transformation — connects to Ketu-MD transition."
    - "Mercury BAV on Capricorn (10H) = 5 (good). MD lord supports the career house where he sits."
    - "Mercury BAV on Aquarius (11H) = 2 (WEAK). MD lord gives minimal support to gains-house — converges with 11H SAV=23 and Badhaka findings."
    financial_significance: HIGH
    interpretation: >
      Mercury (MD lord) maximally supports 2H (direct wealth) and 8H (transformation) but minimally
      supports 11H (gains). This means: under Mercury MD, wealth accumulates more readily through
      direct-savings and transformation-events than through network-gains channels. Aligns with
      the 12H-redirect prescription and the Ketu-MD transition architecture.

  jupiter_bav_highlights:
    - "Jupiter BAV on Libra (7H) = 7 (Jupiter's HIGHEST). The dharma-planet gives maximum bindu-support to the Sasha Yoga / Raja Yoga house, despite BVB.7 being Bhavabala-weakest. ANOTHER PARADOX: Jupiter provides the strongest planetary BAV support to the weakest Bhavabala house."
    - "Jupiter BAV on Capricorn (10H) = 6 (strong). Jupiter supports the career-density axis."
    - "Jupiter BAV on Sagittarius (9H) = 4 (moderate). Jupiter in own sign gets moderate self-support."
    financial_significance: HIGH
    interpretation: >
      Jupiter's strongest BAV is on the 7H — the Raja Yoga seat. Jupiter's BAV partially compensates
      for 7H's Bhavabala weakness. When Jupiter transits Libra (distant — not in 36-month window)
      or aspects Libra (7th aspect from Aries hits Libra — Saturn in Aries mid-2026 to 2028 means
      Saturn+Jupiter would need co-transit patterns for this), the 7H receives maximum Jupiter support.
      During Jupiter Cancer exaltation (Jun-Oct 2026), Jupiter's 7th aspect hits Capricorn (10H),
      NOT Libra — so the Cancer transit doesn't activate this BAV finding directly.

  saturn_bav_highlights:
    - "Saturn BAV on Capricorn (10H) = 2 (WEAK). Saturn gives minimal support to his OWN 10H. Converges with CTR.01 — Saturn's delivery on his own career-house is bindu-impaired."
    - "Saturn BAV on Aquarius (11H) = 4 (moderate). Saturn moderately supports his own gains-house."
    - "Saturn BAV on Pisces (12H) = 2 (WEAK). Saturn gives minimal support to the wealth-reservoir."
    - "Saturn BAV on Libra (7H) = 4 (moderate). Saturn moderately supports his own tenancy-house."
    financial_significance: HIGH
    interpretation: >
      Saturn gives weak-to-moderate BAV support to ALL three of his most critical houses (10H, 11H, 12H).
      This is the BAV-level expression of the Shuddha Pinda #7 finding — Saturn's bindu-floor is
      thin everywhere he matters. Combined with the Badhaka finding, this confirms that Saturn-mediated
      delivery requires disproportionate effort for every unit of outcome.

  transit_prediction_bav_thresholds:
    description: "Classical rule: planet transiting a sign where it has ≥5 BAV gives favorable results; ≤2 BAV gives difficult results"
    key_transit_BAV_2026_2028:
      - "Jupiter transit Cancer (Jun-Oct 2026): Jupiter BAV on Cancer = 4 (moderate, NOT ≥5). Jupiter's exaltation transit has moderate BAV support — not peak. The exaltation dignity partially compensates."
      - "Saturn transit Pisces (retro 2026): Saturn BAV on Pisces = 2 (WEAK ≤2). Saturn's Pisces transit is BAV-difficult. Confirms need for Iron Ring pacification."
      - "Saturn transit Aries (2026-2028): Saturn BAV on Aries = 4 (moderate). Saturn in Aries is BAV-moderate."
      - "Rahu transit Capricorn (Dec 2026 onward): Rahu not included in classical BAV. SAV.Capricorn = 26 (below average). Moderate support."
    financial_significance: MEDIUM
```

```yaml
shadbala_component_key_findings:

  venus_dig_bala_near_zero:
    value: "Venus Dig Bala = 4.60 Virupas"
    context: "Venus receives maximum Dig Bala (60) in 4H (Cancer). Venus is in 9H (Sagittarius). Distance from optimal = maximum displacement."
    significance: HIGH
    interpretation: >
      Venus's Dig Bala is the SINGLE LARGEST contributor to Venus's overall weakness. Venus
      is directionally maximally displaced from her optimal seat. The 4th house (home, comfort,
      mother, inner peace) is where Venus would be directionally strongest; she sits in the 9th
      (foreign, dharma, travel — directionally weakest zone for Venus). This means Venus-signified
      outcomes (wealth, relationships, Ishta-Devata intercession) are directionally mis-aligned:
      the planet that should deliver material comfort and wealth-accumulation is pointing toward
      dharma-foreign-teaching rather than toward home-comfort-savings. This perfectly explains
      WHY the chart routes wealth through 12H-foreign-compounding rather than through 2H-family-
      savings: Venus's directional orientation points AWAY from 2H/4H accumulation.

  moon_hora_bala_maximum:
    value: "Moon Hora Bala = 60 Virupas (MAXIMUM)"
    context: "Born during Moon's hora (time-segment ruled by Moon)"
    significance: MEDIUM
    interpretation: >
      Moon as AK receives maximum temporal support from the birth-hora. This specifically
      strengthens Moon's operational delivery: the soul-signifier's temporal foundation is
      strong. Moon's weakness (Vimsopaka rank 7, Mrat Avastha) is partially offset by this
      temporal-strength. The hora-support is structural-background, not event-driven.

    context: "Born on Sunday = Sun's weekday"
    significance: MEDIUM

    significance: MEDIUM

      Jupiter receives the highest temporal-sub-component total of any planet. Jupiter is
      temporally-favored: the dharma-wealth-terminal-dispositor operates with strong temporal
      grounding. This partially offsets Jupiter's Uccha Bala weakness (rank 7).

  all_drik_bala_negative:
    observation: "Every planet has negative Drik Bala (aspectual load). Sun = -35.08 (MOST negative), Jupiter = -6.98 (LEAST negative)."
    significance: LOW
    interpretation: >
      No planet receives net-benefic aspectual support. The chart's aspect geometry is
      predominantly martial/malefic (Mars+Saturn aspects dominate). This is a chart-wide
      condition rather than a planet-specific finding — it means all planets operate under
      malefic aspectual pressure. Saturn and Mars as the chart's primary aspect-casters
      create the dominant aspectual load.
```

```yaml
  fortress_architecture:

    bahya_exterior_moat: "Mars + Saturn + Rahu — 7H pair + 2H Rahu as outer defense"

    intelligence (Sun+Mercury) as inner court → dharmic-wealth (Jupiter+Venus) as walls →
    partnerships and unconventional channels (Mars+Saturn+Rahu) as moat. The career axis is
    MORE PROTECTED than the wealth-dharma axis, which is MORE PROTECTED than the partnership
    axis. This means: career stability is the most structurally resilient domain; wealth-dharma
    is the second-most resilient; partnerships are the LEAST protected (moat = first point
    of external contact). Converges with: 10H Bhavabala rank 3 > 9H rank 5 > 7H rank 12.
  financial_significance: MEDIUM

    the entity that PROTECTS the fortress is also the entity that creates OBSTRUCTION within it.
    The fort lord both shields and constrains.

panchang_birth_forensic:
  combined_reading:
    vara: "Sunday (Surya/Agni) — authority, fire, leadership"
    tithi: "Shukla Tritiya (Jaya = Victory) — conquers obstacles through effort"
    yoga: "Shiva (Auspicious) — clarity, respect, calm mind"
    karana: "Garija (Earth/Productive) — good for foundations, building, productive work"
    nakshatra: "Purva Bhadrapada (Ugra/Fierce) — transformative intensity, spiritual fire"
  synthesis: >
    The birth Panchang combines authority (Sunday) + victory-through-effort (Shukla Tritiya) +
    auspicious clarity (Shiva Yoga) + productive foundation-building (Garija Karana) + fierce
    transformative intensity (Purva Bhadrapada). This PERFECTLY matches the chart's structural
    architecture: Saraswati-knowledge-wealth (clarity + foundations) built through authority-
    effort (Sunday + Jaya tithi) with transformative intensity (Ugra nakshatra). The Panchang
    DNA and the chart architecture are in deep alignment — the native's temporal birth-
    fingerprint specifically supports the structural reading.
  financial_significance: MEDIUM
  dagdha_rashis_financial_note: >
    Leo (5H) and Capricorn (10H) are Dagdha (burnt) for this native. The 5H (creativity/
    speculation) and 10H (career) carry Dagdha vulnerability. For financial purposes: avoid
    initiating new ventures when transit Moon is in Leo or Capricorn (approximately 4-5 days
    per month total). Career and creative-speculative ventures are specifically subject to
    Dagdha-Rashi timing restrictions.
```

### RPT.AUD.09 — Complete Argala (Jaimini Intervention) Map

**[Audit Pass 3, 2026-04-16]**

```yaml
argala_complete_map:
  description: >
    Argala = Jaimini's intervention mechanism. Planets in the 2nd, 4th, 11th, and 5th
    from a house provide Argala (support/intervention). Virodha (counter): 12th counters
    2nd-Argala, 10th counters 4th-Argala, 3rd counters 11th-Argala. Argala prevails when
    the Argala-providers outnumber the Virodha-providers.

  house_argala_summary:
    - house: "1H (Lagna / Self)"
      argala: "Rahu (2nd from 1H=Taurus), Moon (11th from 1H=Aquarius)"
      strength: MODERATE
    - house: "2H (Wealth)"
      argala: "NONE significant"
      strength: MINIMAL
      financial_note: "The direct-wealth house is ARGALA-UNSUPPORTED — independently confirms Bhavabala rank 11 weakness via Jaimini mechanics"
    - house: "3H (Skills/Communication)"
      argala: "NONE"
      strength: MINIMAL
    - house: "4H (Home/Property)"
      argala: "Mars+Saturn (4th from 4H=Libra), Rahu (11th from 4H=Taurus)"
      strength: MODERATE
      note: "Property supported by authority-partnership dynamics"
    - house: "5H (Creativity/Speculation)"
      argala: "Ketu (4th from 5H=Scorpio)"
      strength: MINIMAL
    - house: "6H (Enemies/Service)"
      argala: "Mars+Saturn (2nd from 6H=Libra), Jupiter+Venus (4th from 6H=Sagittarius)"
      strength: DOUBLE STRONG
      note: "Strong tools against obstacles — the native is WELL-RESOURCED against enemies"
    - house: "7H (Partners)"
      argala: "Ketu (2nd=Scorpio), Sun+Mercury (4th=Capricorn), Moon (5th=Aquarius)"
      strength: MODERATE-STRONG
      financial_note: "Despite BVB rank 12 (weakest), 7H receives strong Argala from career axis (Sun+Mercury). Career FEEDS partnerships through Argala even though the house's own substance is weak."
      new_finding: TRUE
    - house: "8H (Transformation)"
      argala: "Jupiter+Venus (2nd=Sag) CONTESTED by Mars+Saturn Virodha (12th=Libra); Moon (4th=Aquarius)"
      strength: CONTESTED
    - house: "9H (Dharma/Fortune)"
      argala: "Sun+Mercury (2nd=Capricorn), Mars+Saturn (11th=Libra)"
      strength: DOUBLE STRONG
      financial_note: "The Lakshmi/Maha Dhana seat receives the STRONGEST Argala of any house. Career axis (Sun+Mercury) AND authority-partnerships (Mars+Saturn) BOTH feed the dharma-wealth seat. This is an INDEPENDENT Jaimini confirmation that all wealth-relevant houses structurally feed into 9H."
      new_finding: TRUE
    - house: "10H (Career)"
      argala: "Moon (2nd=Aquarius), Ketu (4th=Scorpio)"
      strength: MODERATE
    - house: "11H (Gains)"
      argala: "Jupiter+Venus (11th=Sagittarius); Rahu (4th=Taurus) CONTESTED by Ketu Virodha"
      strength: MODERATE
    - house: "12H (Foreign/Accumulation)"
      argala: "Sun+Mercury (11th=Capricorn)"
      strength: STRONG
      financial_note: "Career axis provides DIRECT Argala to the wealth-reservoir. INDEPENDENTLY CONFIRMED across Pass 1 and now mapped in full context."

  architectural_synthesis: >
    The complete Argala map reveals a clear financial-flow architecture:
    (1) 9H receives DOUBLE-STRONG Argala = the dharma-wealth seat is the most supported house
    (2) 12H receives STRONG Argala from career = the wealth-reservoir is career-fed
    (3) 7H receives moderate-strong Argala despite BVB weakness = career compensates partnership weakness
    (4) 2H receives NO Argala = direct-wealth channel is structurally unsupported
    (5) 6H receives DOUBLE-STRONG Argala = strong defense against obstacles
    
    FLOW: Career (10H) → feeds 9H dharma-wealth AND 12H accumulation
          Partnerships (7H) → feeds 9H dharma-wealth
          Direct-wealth (2H) → bypassed (no Argala)
    
    This PERFECTLY maps onto the Parashari-derived §5.4 redirect-architecture reading.
    Three independent classical frameworks now converge on the same conclusion:
    (A) Parashari Bhavabala: 12H rank 1 > 10H rank 3 > 9H rank 5 >> 2H rank 11
    (B) Jaimini Argala: 9H double-strong > 12H strong > 7H moderate-strong > 2H zero
    (C) Maha Dhana dispositor chain: all wealth lords route through Venus → Jupiter (9H)
```

### RPT.AUD.13 — Narayana Dasha Computation (Estimated)

```yaml
narayana_dasha:
  computation_method: "Sanjay Rath / K.N. Rao Narayana Dasha. Aries = Chara (movable) Lagna → start from Lagna, move zodiacally forward. Duration = forward-count from sign to lord (for odd signs), backward-count (for even signs). Lord-in-own-sign = 12 years."
  confidence: 0.65 (MODERATE — computation follows standard rules but counting conventions vary between traditions; requires verification against dedicated Narayana Dasha software)

  computation_table:
    - sign: Aries (odd)
      lord: Mars (Libra, sign 7)
      count: "Forward from Aries to Libra = 7"
      duration: 7 years

      February 2026. This means a FOURTH dasha system now points to the 7H/Libra axis as
      the current operational focus:
      
      (1) Vimshottari: Mercury-Saturn AD (Saturn sits IN Libra 7H)

      indicators point to 7H Libra as the current operative axis.
      
      For financial purposes: the 2026-2029 period is SPECIFICALLY configured for partnership-
      wealth, contract-based-income, and authority-through-counterpart mechanisms. This
      reinforces §5.3 (Hidden Raja Yoga) as not merely a structural finding but a TEMPORALLY-
      ACTIVATED finding for the current window.
      
    caveat: >
      This computation has 0.65 confidence due to counting-convention variability. If the
      duration computation is off by ±1 year per sign (a common variance between traditions),
      the Libra period could start as early as 2025 or as late as 2027. The KEY claim —
      that Libra/7H is the current Narayana period — holds across most plausible variants,
      but the exact start/end years should be verified with dedicated software.
```

## §D.7 — Intervention Leverage Map

### RPT.INT.00 — Framing and Constraints

```yaml
scope: "Interventions are listed ONLY if they are (a) mechanically traceable to v6.0 IDs or classical Jyotish rules, and (b) have an identifiable leverage vector into the current chart-architecture."
exclusions:
  - "No intervention is recommended that relies on unverifiable mystical claims disconnected from chart-derived reasoning."
  - "No intervention is recommended that conflicts with the native's existing protocol established in conversation memory, unless the v6.0 data contradicts that protocol (in which case the contradiction is flagged explicitly)."
  - "Medical, legal, and financial interventions are outside this report's remit. All recommendations are astrological-ritual interventions only."
priority_ordering_criteria:
  - Structural_leverage: Does the intervention act on a top-CVI point (CVG.01–08)?
  - Dasha_activation: Does it align with currently-active dasha lords or imminent transitions?
  - Transit_convergence: Does it align with DAS-critical-tier months (D.5 heatmap)?
  - Native_operational_compatibility: Is it executable at Bhubaneswar given native's operational context?
  - Reversibility: Low-cost / low-risk interventions preferred first; high-commitment interventions reserved for high-confidence windows
```

#### INT.01.B — Timing-leverage rationale

The window **2026-04-19 to 2027-01-05** is operationally a "planting period" — Saturn AD is active, but pre-harvest. The window **2027-01-05 to 2027-08-21** is the "harvest window" per the Chara Pada transition. The window **2027-08-21 onwards** is Ketu MD — a fundamentally different regime where accumulated-material harvest risks dissolution unless secured pre-transition.

This yields a strong implication:

> **Major financial structures (contracts, account-openings, foreign-earning commitments) should be either completed pre-2027-08-21 or deferred until Ketu MD has stabilized (approximately 2028-Q2 onwards after Ketu transit has entered Gemini/Sagittarius mode).**

```yaml
  planetary_state:
    - Jupiter: Cancer (exalted — entered 2026-06-02)
    - Mercury: Cancer (combust cycle — enters combust ~Jul 14; combustion is a caveat, see below)
    - Sun: Cancer
    - Mars: transiting
    - Rahu: Aquarius (pre-Dec-5 ingress)
    - Ketu: Leo
    - Saturn: Aries retrograde
    - Moon: computed via ephemeris
  dasha_state:
    Vimshottari: Mer-MD / Sat-AD / (PD and SD require exact computation)
    Yogini: Bhadrika (Mercury) — 5 months before Ulka transition
    Chara: Sco-Lib (7.5 months before Sco-Vir transition)
  tithi_nakshatra:
    Tithi: Ashadha Shukla Dwitiya (by definition — this is what defines Rath Yatra)
    Nakshatra: requires ephemeris confirmation (typically Punarvasu or Pushya per Rath-Yatra-date canonical calculations)
  devata_alignment:
    - Jagannath: Ashadha Shukla Dwitiya is the scripturally-mandated day
    - Lakshmi: Jupiter-Cancer-exalt is a Lakshmi-favorable atmospheric condition (Jupiter = Lakshmi-consort-Vishnu-guru)
    - Sudarshana: Vishnu-chakra form — Saturn-AD aspect supports protective-invocation
  caveats:
    - Jupiter combusts Jul 14 2026 (2 days before Rath Yatra). Mercury also approaching combust cycle.
    - Combust-Jupiter is a real atmospheric caveat BUT: Rath Yatra is fixed-date scriptural — the devata's own timing overrides planetary-atmospheric conditions for Jagannath-specific worship.
    - The Homam should explicitly include Brihaspati-gayatri and Surya-gayatri as pre-homa invocations to mitigate combust-Jupiter and empower the Sun (whose hora/tithi may or may not align on Jul 16).
```

#### RED.02.C — Resolution of Mercury Rashi-vs-Chalit discrepancy

Per memory: v6.0 reports (or prior reports reported) an inconsistency on Mercury's Rashi vs Chalit house placement. v6.0 excerpts consumed show:

```
Mercury: Rashi sign Capricorn — Rashi house 10 (Cap is 10th sign from Aries Lagna)
Mercury: Chalit — depends on exact longitude vs cusps
```

v6.0 data point: Mercury is the closest-to-cusp planet (2.14° from 10H cusp). This means Mercury is VERY CLOSE to cusp, and could fall into 9H or 10H depending on cusp-calculation method.

```yaml
patch_for_MercuryCuspAmbiguity:
  - status: Mercury is BORDER-case between 9H and 10H
  - this_report_uses: Rashi house = 10H (standard house = sign assignment from Aries Lagna)
  - Chalit calculation would depend on Placidus/Bhava-Chalit method (v6.0 should specify — appears to use Bhava-Chalit method yielding Mercury in 10H Chalit as well, but this should be confirmed)
  - implication_if_9H: Mercury-in-9H would make it Jupiter-9L-conjunction analog, strengthening 9H and transferring Budh-Aditya yoga to 9H axis; Foreign-architecture interpretation would INTENSIFY (9H = long-journeys = foreign)
  - implication_if_10H: Mercury supports career-density-10H-cluster; Budh-Aditya at 10H = classical karmic-success signature
  - recommendation: Both interpretations yield pro-native-goal outcomes; the precise cusp-method choice is low-stakes for intervention-selection
```

```yaml
  - Venus (Ishta ruler) Shadbala 4.60 below min — EMPHASIZED in DEV.01 (NOT hidden)

  - Sade Sati active — explicitly flagged throughout (Saturn-AD is described as bimodal, not purely-positive)
  - Eclipse hits on natal Sun Aug 6 2028 during Ketu-Sun AD — flagged as HIGH-CAUTION
  - Ketu MD regime change 2027-08-21 — flagged as regime-break requiring pre-position
bias_conclusion: "Report appears to PRESERVE obstacles rather than mask them. The confirmation-bias risk is not acute; however, the native's protocol-commitment (from memory) may selectively filter-in pro-goal portions of this report. Native should explicitly re-read the CONTRA-goal sections (HSE.02, RED.03.A counter-list) during strategic decisions."
```

```yaml
    note: "The framing is conservative — 'regime change' implies shift in character, not necessarily loss or gain direction."
  - claim: "Eclipse Aug 6 2028 on natal Sun during Ketu-Sun AD = high-caution"
    status: ACCEPTABLE
    note: "Multi-factor convergence (eclipse + conjunction + dasha-AD-of-same-planet) is classically a strong activation. Framing as 'caution' is appropriate."
  - claim: "Immense/immediate/impeccable/irreversible financial outcome achievable"
    status: REPORT-DOES-NOT-MAKE-THIS-CLAIM
    note: "Report addresses the native's architecture for financial leverage but does not promise outcome-magnitude. The four adjectives are native's goal-framing, not chart-interpretation."
```

## §D.9 — Master Cross-Reference Index

### RPT.XRF.00 — Index framing

This index provides a lookup from every analytical finding to (a) the v6.0 data IDs it consumed, (b) the classical rules invoked, (c) the layers it traversed in the 7-layer depth ladder, and (d) related RPT.* findings.

This enables any user or downstream analyst to audit the full derivation chain for any claim in this report.

